\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{1 \textcolor{comment}{/* stb\_image -\/ v2.27 -\/ public domain image loader -\/ http://nothings.org/stb}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2 \textcolor{comment}{                                  no warranty implied; use at your own risk}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4 \textcolor{comment}{   Do this:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5 \textcolor{comment}{      \#define STB\_IMAGE\_IMPLEMENTATION}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6 \textcolor{comment}{   before you include this file in *one* C or C++ file to create the implementation.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{7 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8 \textcolor{comment}{   // i.e. it should look like this:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{9 \textcolor{comment}{   \#include ...}}
\DoxyCodeLine{10 \textcolor{comment}{   \#include ...}}
\DoxyCodeLine{11 \textcolor{comment}{   \#include ...}}
\DoxyCodeLine{12 \textcolor{comment}{   \#define STB\_IMAGE\_IMPLEMENTATION}}
\DoxyCodeLine{13 \textcolor{comment}{   \#include "{}stb\_image.h"{}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{14 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{15 \textcolor{comment}{   You can \#define STBI\_ASSERT(x) before the \#include to avoid using assert.h.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{16 \textcolor{comment}{   And \#define STBI\_MALLOC, STBI\_REALLOC, and STBI\_FREE to avoid using malloc,realloc,free}}
\DoxyCodeLine{17 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{18 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{19 \textcolor{comment}{   QUICK NOTES:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{20 \textcolor{comment}{      Primarily of interest to game developers and other people who can}}
\DoxyCodeLine{21 \textcolor{comment}{          avoid problematic images and only need the trivial interface}}
\DoxyCodeLine{22 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{23 \textcolor{comment}{      JPEG baseline \& progressive (12 bpc/arithmetic not supported, same as stock IJG lib)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{24 \textcolor{comment}{      PNG 1/2/4/8/16-\/bit-\/per-\/channel}}
\DoxyCodeLine{25 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{26 \textcolor{comment}{      TGA (not sure what subset, if a subset)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{27 \textcolor{comment}{      BMP non-\/1bpp, non-\/RLE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{28 \textcolor{comment}{      PSD (composited view only, no extra channels, 8/16 bit-\/per-\/channel)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{29 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{30 \textcolor{comment}{      GIF (*comp always reports as 4-\/channel)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{31 \textcolor{comment}{      HDR (radiance rgbE format)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{32 \textcolor{comment}{      PIC (Softimage PIC)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{33 \textcolor{comment}{      PNM (PPM and PGM binary only)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{34 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{35 \textcolor{comment}{      Animated GIF still needs a proper API, but here's one way to do it:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{36 \textcolor{comment}{          http://gist.github.com/urraka/685d9a6340b26b830d49}}
\DoxyCodeLine{37 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{38 \textcolor{comment}{      -\/ decode from memory or through FILE (define STBI\_NO\_STDIO to remove code)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{39 \textcolor{comment}{      -\/ decode from arbitrary I/O callbacks}}
\DoxyCodeLine{40 \textcolor{comment}{      -\/ SIMD acceleration on x86/x64 (SSE2) and ARM (NEON)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{41 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{42 \textcolor{comment}{   Full documentation under "{}DOCUMENTATION"{} below.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{43 \textcolor{comment}{}}

\DoxyCodeLine{129 \textcolor{comment}{// DOCUMENTATION}}
\DoxyCodeLine{130 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{131 \textcolor{comment}{// Limitations:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{132 \textcolor{comment}{//    -\/ no 12-\/bit-\/per-\/channel JPEG}}
\DoxyCodeLine{133 \textcolor{comment}{//    -\/ no JPEGs with arithmetic coding}}
\DoxyCodeLine{134 \textcolor{comment}{//    -\/ GIF always returns *comp=4}}
\DoxyCodeLine{135 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{136 \textcolor{comment}{// Basic usage (see HDR discussion below for HDR usage):}}
\DoxyCodeLine{137 \textcolor{comment}{//    int x,y,n;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{138 \textcolor{comment}{//    unsigned char *data = stbi\_load(filename, \&x, \&y, \&n, 0);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{139 \textcolor{comment}{//    // ... process data if not NULL ...}}
\DoxyCodeLine{140 \textcolor{comment}{//    // ... x = width, y = height, n = \# 8-\/bit components per pixel ...}}
\DoxyCodeLine{141 \textcolor{comment}{//    // ... replace '0' with '1'..'4' to force that many components per pixel}}
\DoxyCodeLine{142 \textcolor{comment}{//    // ... but 'n' will always be the number that it would have been if you said 0}}
\DoxyCodeLine{143 \textcolor{comment}{//    stbi\_image\_free(data)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{144 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{145 \textcolor{comment}{// Standard parameters:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{146 \textcolor{comment}{//    int *x                 -\/-\/ outputs image width in pixels}}
\DoxyCodeLine{147 \textcolor{comment}{//    int *y                 -\/-\/ outputs image height in pixels}}
\DoxyCodeLine{148 \textcolor{comment}{//    int *channels\_in\_file  -\/-\/ outputs \# of image components in image file}}
\DoxyCodeLine{149 \textcolor{comment}{//    int desired\_channels   -\/-\/ if non-\/zero, \# of image components requested in result}}
\DoxyCodeLine{150 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{151 \textcolor{comment}{// The return value from an image loader is an 'unsigned char *' which points}}
\DoxyCodeLine{152 \textcolor{comment}{// to the pixel data, or NULL on an allocation failure or if the image is}}
\DoxyCodeLine{153 \textcolor{comment}{// corrupt or invalid. The pixel data consists of *y scanlines of *x pixels,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{154 \textcolor{comment}{// with each pixel consisting of N interleaved 8-\/bit components; the first}}
\DoxyCodeLine{155 \textcolor{comment}{// pixel pointed to is top-\/left-\/most in the image. There is no padding between}}
\DoxyCodeLine{156 \textcolor{comment}{// image scanlines or between pixels, regardless of format. The number of}}
\DoxyCodeLine{157 \textcolor{comment}{// components N is 'desired\_channels' if desired\_channels is non-\/zero, or}}
\DoxyCodeLine{158 \textcolor{comment}{// *channels\_in\_file otherwise. If desired\_channels is non-\/zero,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{159 \textcolor{comment}{// *channels\_in\_file has the number of components that \_would\_ have been}}
\DoxyCodeLine{160 \textcolor{comment}{// output otherwise. E.g. if you set desired\_channels to 4, you will always}}
\DoxyCodeLine{161 \textcolor{comment}{// get RGBA output, but you can check *channels\_in\_file to see if it's trivially}}
\DoxyCodeLine{162 \textcolor{comment}{// opaque because e.g. there were only 3 channels in the source image.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{163 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{164 \textcolor{comment}{// An output image with N components has the following components interleaved}}
\DoxyCodeLine{165 \textcolor{comment}{// in this order in each pixel:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{166 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{167 \textcolor{comment}{//     N=\#comp     components}}
\DoxyCodeLine{168 \textcolor{comment}{//       1           grey}}
\DoxyCodeLine{169 \textcolor{comment}{//       2           grey, alpha}}
\DoxyCodeLine{170 \textcolor{comment}{//       3           red, green, blue}}
\DoxyCodeLine{171 \textcolor{comment}{//       4           red, green, blue, alpha}}
\DoxyCodeLine{172 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{173 \textcolor{comment}{// If image loading fails for any reason, the return value will be NULL,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{174 \textcolor{comment}{// and *x, *y, *channels\_in\_file will be unchanged. The function}}
\DoxyCodeLine{175 \textcolor{comment}{// stbi\_failure\_reason() can be queried for an extremely brief, end-\/user}}
\DoxyCodeLine{176 \textcolor{comment}{// unfriendly explanation of why the load failed. Define STBI\_NO\_FAILURE\_STRINGS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{177 \textcolor{comment}{// to avoid compiling these strings at all, and STBI\_FAILURE\_USERMSG to get slightly}}
\DoxyCodeLine{178 \textcolor{comment}{// more user-\/friendly ones.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{179 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{180 \textcolor{comment}{// Paletted PNG, BMP, GIF, and PIC images are automatically depalettized.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{181 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{182 \textcolor{comment}{// To query the width, height and component count of an image without having to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{183 \textcolor{comment}{// decode the full file, you can use the stbi\_info family of functions:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{184 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{185 \textcolor{comment}{//   int x,y,n,ok;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{186 \textcolor{comment}{//   ok = stbi\_info(filename, \&x, \&y, \&n);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{187 \textcolor{comment}{//   // returns ok=1 and sets x, y, n if image is a supported format,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{188 \textcolor{comment}{//   // 0 otherwise.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{189 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{190 \textcolor{comment}{// Note that stb\_image pervasively uses ints in its public API for sizes,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{191 \textcolor{comment}{// including sizes of memory buffers. This is now part of the API and thus}}
\DoxyCodeLine{192 \textcolor{comment}{// hard to change without causing breakage. As a result, the various image}}
\DoxyCodeLine{193 \textcolor{comment}{// loaders all have certain limits on image size; these differ somewhat}}
\DoxyCodeLine{194 \textcolor{comment}{// by format but generally boil down to either just under 2GB or just under}}
\DoxyCodeLine{195 \textcolor{comment}{// 1GB. When the decoded image would be larger than this, stb\_image decoding}}
\DoxyCodeLine{196 \textcolor{comment}{// will fail.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{197 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{198 \textcolor{comment}{// Additionally, stb\_image will reject image files that have any of their}}
\DoxyCodeLine{199 \textcolor{comment}{// dimensions set to a larger value than the configurable STBI\_MAX\_DIMENSIONS,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{200 \textcolor{comment}{// which defaults to 2**24 = 16777216 pixels. Due to the above memory limit,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{201 \textcolor{comment}{// the only way to have an image with such dimensions load correctly}}
\DoxyCodeLine{202 \textcolor{comment}{// is for it to have a rather extreme aspect ratio. Either way, the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{203 \textcolor{comment}{// assumption here is that such larger images are likely to be malformed}}
\DoxyCodeLine{204 \textcolor{comment}{// or malicious. If you do need to load an image with individual dimensions}}
\DoxyCodeLine{205 \textcolor{comment}{// larger than that, and it still fits in the overall size limit, you can}}
\DoxyCodeLine{206 \textcolor{comment}{// \#define STBI\_MAX\_DIMENSIONS on your own to be something larger.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{207 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{208 \textcolor{comment}{// ===========================================================================}}
\DoxyCodeLine{209 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{210 \textcolor{comment}{// UNICODE:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{211 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{212 \textcolor{comment}{//   If compiling for Windows and you wish to use Unicode filenames, compile}}
\DoxyCodeLine{213 \textcolor{comment}{//   with}}
\DoxyCodeLine{214 \textcolor{comment}{//       \#define STBI\_WINDOWS\_UTF8}}
\DoxyCodeLine{215 \textcolor{comment}{//   and pass utf8-\/encoded filenames. Call stbi\_convert\_wchar\_to\_utf8 to convert}}
\DoxyCodeLine{216 \textcolor{comment}{//   Windows wchar\_t filenames to utf8.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{217 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{218 \textcolor{comment}{// ===========================================================================}}
\DoxyCodeLine{219 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{220 \textcolor{comment}{// Philosophy}}
\DoxyCodeLine{221 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{222 \textcolor{comment}{// stb libraries are designed with the following priorities:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{223 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{224 \textcolor{comment}{//    1. easy to use}}
\DoxyCodeLine{225 \textcolor{comment}{//    2. easy to maintain}}
\DoxyCodeLine{226 \textcolor{comment}{//    3. good performance}}
\DoxyCodeLine{227 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{228 \textcolor{comment}{// Sometimes I let "{}good performance"{} creep up in priority over "{}easy to maintain"{},}}
\DoxyCodeLine{229 \textcolor{comment}{// and for best performance I may provide less-\/easy-\/to-\/use APIs that give higher}}
\DoxyCodeLine{230 \textcolor{comment}{// performance, in addition to the easy-\/to-\/use ones. Nevertheless, it's important}}
\DoxyCodeLine{231 \textcolor{comment}{// to keep in mind that from the standpoint of you, a client of this library,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{232 \textcolor{comment}{// all you care about is \#1 and \#3, and stb libraries DO NOT emphasize \#3 above all.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{233 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{234 \textcolor{comment}{// Some secondary priorities arise directly from the first two, some of which}}
\DoxyCodeLine{235 \textcolor{comment}{// provide more explicit reasons why performance can't be emphasized.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{236 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{237 \textcolor{comment}{//    -\/ Portable ("{}ease of use"{})}}
\DoxyCodeLine{238 \textcolor{comment}{//    -\/ Small source code footprint ("{}easy to maintain"{})}}
\DoxyCodeLine{239 \textcolor{comment}{//    -\/ No dependencies ("{}ease of use"{})}}
\DoxyCodeLine{240 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{241 \textcolor{comment}{// ===========================================================================}}
\DoxyCodeLine{242 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{243 \textcolor{comment}{// I/O callbacks}}
\DoxyCodeLine{244 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{245 \textcolor{comment}{// I/O callbacks allow you to read from arbitrary sources, like packaged}}
\DoxyCodeLine{246 \textcolor{comment}{// files or some other source. Data read from callbacks are processed}}
\DoxyCodeLine{247 \textcolor{comment}{// through a small internal buffer (currently 128 bytes) to try to reduce}}
\DoxyCodeLine{248 \textcolor{comment}{// overhead.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{249 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{250 \textcolor{comment}{// The three functions you must define are "{}read"{} (reads some bytes of data),}}
\DoxyCodeLine{251 \textcolor{comment}{// "{}skip"{} (skips some bytes of data), "{}eof"{} (reports if the stream is at the end).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{252 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{253 \textcolor{comment}{// ===========================================================================}}
\DoxyCodeLine{254 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{255 \textcolor{comment}{// SIMD support}}
\DoxyCodeLine{256 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{257 \textcolor{comment}{// The JPEG decoder will try to automatically use SIMD kernels on x86 when}}
\DoxyCodeLine{258 \textcolor{comment}{// supported by the compiler. For ARM Neon support, you must explicitly}}
\DoxyCodeLine{259 \textcolor{comment}{// request it.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{260 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{261 \textcolor{comment}{// (The old do-\/it-\/yourself SIMD API is no longer supported in the current}}
\DoxyCodeLine{262 \textcolor{comment}{// code.)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{263 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{264 \textcolor{comment}{// On x86, SSE2 will automatically be used when available based on a run-\/time}}
\DoxyCodeLine{265 \textcolor{comment}{// test; if not, the generic C versions are used as a fall-\/back. On ARM targets,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{266 \textcolor{comment}{// the typical path is to have separate builds for NEON and non-\/NEON devices}}
\DoxyCodeLine{267 \textcolor{comment}{// (at least this is true for iOS and Android). Therefore, the NEON support is}}
\DoxyCodeLine{268 \textcolor{comment}{// toggled by a build flag: define STBI\_NEON to get NEON loops.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{269 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{270 \textcolor{comment}{// If for some reason you do not want to use any of SIMD code, or if}}
\DoxyCodeLine{271 \textcolor{comment}{// you have issues compiling it, you can disable it entirely by}}
\DoxyCodeLine{272 \textcolor{comment}{// defining STBI\_NO\_SIMD.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{273 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{274 \textcolor{comment}{// ===========================================================================}}
\DoxyCodeLine{275 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{276 \textcolor{comment}{// HDR image support   (disable by defining STBI\_NO\_HDR)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{277 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{278 \textcolor{comment}{// stb\_image supports loading HDR images in general, and currently the Radiance}}
\DoxyCodeLine{279 \textcolor{comment}{// .HDR file format specifically. You can still load any file through the existing}}
\DoxyCodeLine{280 \textcolor{comment}{// interface; if you attempt to load an HDR file, it will be automatically remapped}}
\DoxyCodeLine{281 \textcolor{comment}{// to LDR, assuming gamma 2.2 and an arbitrary scale factor defaulting to 1;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{282 \textcolor{comment}{// both of these constants can be reconfigured through this interface:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{283 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{284 \textcolor{comment}{//     stbi\_hdr\_to\_ldr\_gamma(2.2f);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{285 \textcolor{comment}{//     stbi\_hdr\_to\_ldr\_scale(1.0f);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{286 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{287 \textcolor{comment}{// (note, do not use \_inverse\_ constants; stbi\_image will invert them}}
\DoxyCodeLine{288 \textcolor{comment}{// appropriately).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{289 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{290 \textcolor{comment}{// Additionally, there is a new, parallel interface for loading files as}}
\DoxyCodeLine{291 \textcolor{comment}{// (linear) floats to preserve the full dynamic range:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{292 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{293 \textcolor{comment}{//    float *data = stbi\_loadf(filename, \&x, \&y, \&n, 0);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{294 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{295 \textcolor{comment}{// If you load LDR images through this interface, those images will}}
\DoxyCodeLine{296 \textcolor{comment}{// be promoted to floating point values, run through the inverse of}}
\DoxyCodeLine{297 \textcolor{comment}{// constants corresponding to the above:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{298 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{299 \textcolor{comment}{//     stbi\_ldr\_to\_hdr\_scale(1.0f);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{300 \textcolor{comment}{//     stbi\_ldr\_to\_hdr\_gamma(2.2f);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{301 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{302 \textcolor{comment}{// Finally, given a filename (or an open file or memory block-\/-\/see header}}
\DoxyCodeLine{303 \textcolor{comment}{// file for details) containing image data, you can query for the "{}most}}
\DoxyCodeLine{304 \textcolor{comment}{// appropriate"{} interface to use (that is, whether the image is HDR or}}
\DoxyCodeLine{305 \textcolor{comment}{// not), using:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{306 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{307 \textcolor{comment}{//     stbi\_is\_hdr(char *filename);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{308 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{309 \textcolor{comment}{// ===========================================================================}}
\DoxyCodeLine{310 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{311 \textcolor{comment}{// iPhone PNG support:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{312 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{313 \textcolor{comment}{// We optionally support converting iPhone-\/formatted PNGs (which store}}
\DoxyCodeLine{314 \textcolor{comment}{// premultiplied BGRA) back to RGB, even though they're internally encoded}}
\DoxyCodeLine{315 \textcolor{comment}{// differently. To enable this conversion, call}}
\DoxyCodeLine{316 \textcolor{comment}{// stbi\_convert\_iphone\_png\_to\_rgb(1).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{317 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{318 \textcolor{comment}{// Call stbi\_set\_unpremultiply\_on\_load(1) as well to force a divide per}}
\DoxyCodeLine{319 \textcolor{comment}{// pixel to remove any premultiplied alpha *only* if the image file explicitly}}
\DoxyCodeLine{320 \textcolor{comment}{// says there's premultiplied data (currently only happens in iPhone images,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{321 \textcolor{comment}{// and only if iPhone convert-\/to-\/rgb processing is on).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{322 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{323 \textcolor{comment}{// ===========================================================================}}
\DoxyCodeLine{324 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{325 \textcolor{comment}{// ADDITIONAL CONFIGURATION}}
\DoxyCodeLine{326 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{327 \textcolor{comment}{//  -\/ You can suppress implementation of any of the decoders to reduce}}
\DoxyCodeLine{328 \textcolor{comment}{//    your code footprint by \#defining one or more of the following}}
\DoxyCodeLine{329 \textcolor{comment}{//    symbols before creating the implementation.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{330 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{331 \textcolor{comment}{//        STBI\_NO\_JPEG}}
\DoxyCodeLine{332 \textcolor{comment}{//        STBI\_NO\_PNG}}
\DoxyCodeLine{333 \textcolor{comment}{//        STBI\_NO\_BMP}}
\DoxyCodeLine{334 \textcolor{comment}{//        STBI\_NO\_PSD}}
\DoxyCodeLine{335 \textcolor{comment}{//        STBI\_NO\_TGA}}
\DoxyCodeLine{336 \textcolor{comment}{//        STBI\_NO\_GIF}}
\DoxyCodeLine{337 \textcolor{comment}{//        STBI\_NO\_HDR}}
\DoxyCodeLine{338 \textcolor{comment}{//        STBI\_NO\_PIC}}
\DoxyCodeLine{339 \textcolor{comment}{//        STBI\_NO\_PNM   (.ppm and .pgm)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{340 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{341 \textcolor{comment}{//  -\/ You can request *only* certain decoders and suppress all other ones}}
\DoxyCodeLine{342 \textcolor{comment}{//    (this will be more forward-\/compatible, as addition of new decoders}}
\DoxyCodeLine{343 \textcolor{comment}{//    doesn't require you to disable them explicitly):}}
\DoxyCodeLine{344 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{345 \textcolor{comment}{//        STBI\_ONLY\_JPEG}}
\DoxyCodeLine{346 \textcolor{comment}{//        STBI\_ONLY\_PNG}}
\DoxyCodeLine{347 \textcolor{comment}{//        STBI\_ONLY\_BMP}}
\DoxyCodeLine{348 \textcolor{comment}{//        STBI\_ONLY\_PSD}}
\DoxyCodeLine{349 \textcolor{comment}{//        STBI\_ONLY\_TGA}}
\DoxyCodeLine{350 \textcolor{comment}{//        STBI\_ONLY\_GIF}}
\DoxyCodeLine{351 \textcolor{comment}{//        STBI\_ONLY\_HDR}}
\DoxyCodeLine{352 \textcolor{comment}{//        STBI\_ONLY\_PIC}}
\DoxyCodeLine{353 \textcolor{comment}{//        STBI\_ONLY\_PNM   (.ppm and .pgm)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{354 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{355 \textcolor{comment}{//   -\/ If you use STBI\_NO\_PNG (or \_ONLY\_ without PNG), and you still}}
\DoxyCodeLine{356 \textcolor{comment}{//     want the zlib decoder to be available, \#define STBI\_SUPPORT\_ZLIB}}
\DoxyCodeLine{357 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{358 \textcolor{comment}{//  -\/ If you define STBI\_MAX\_DIMENSIONS, stb\_image will reject images greater}}
\DoxyCodeLine{359 \textcolor{comment}{//    than that size (in either width or height) without further processing.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{360 \textcolor{comment}{//    This is to let programs in the wild set an upper bound to prevent}}
\DoxyCodeLine{361 \textcolor{comment}{//    denial-\/of-\/service attacks on untrusted data, as one could generate a}}
\DoxyCodeLine{362 \textcolor{comment}{//    valid image of gigantic dimensions and force stb\_image to allocate a}}
\DoxyCodeLine{363 \textcolor{comment}{//    huge block of memory and spend disproportionate time decoding it. By}}
\DoxyCodeLine{364 \textcolor{comment}{//    default this is set to (1 << 24), which is 16777216, but that's still}}
\DoxyCodeLine{365 \textcolor{comment}{//    very big.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{366 }
\DoxyCodeLine{367 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#ifndef STBI\_NO\_STDIO}}

\DoxyCodeLine{695 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#if defined(\_\_GNUC\_\_) \&\& defined(STBI\_\_X86\_TARGET) \&\& !defined(\_\_SSE2\_\_) \&\& !defined(STBI\_NO\_SIMD)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{696 \textcolor{comment}{// gcc doesn't support sse2 intrinsics unless you compile with -\/msse2,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{697 \textcolor{comment}{// which in turn means it gets to use SSE2 everywhere. This is unfortunate,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{698 \textcolor{comment}{// but previous attempts to provide the SSE2 functions with runtime}}
\DoxyCodeLine{699 \textcolor{comment}{// detection caused numerous issues. The way architecture extensions are}}
\DoxyCodeLine{700 \textcolor{comment}{// exposed in GCC/Clang is, sadly, not really suited for one-\/file libs.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{701 \textcolor{comment}{// New behavior: if compiled with -\/msse2, we use SSE2 without any}}
\DoxyCodeLine{702 \textcolor{comment}{// detection; if not, we don't use it at all.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{703 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define STBI\_NO\_SIMD}}
\DoxyCodeLine{704 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{705 }
\DoxyCodeLine{706 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#if defined(\_\_MINGW32\_\_) \&\& defined(STBI\_\_X86\_TARGET) \&\& !defined(STBI\_MINGW\_ENABLE\_SSE2) \&\& !defined(STBI\_NO\_SIMD)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{707 \textcolor{comment}{// Note that \_\_MINGW32\_\_ doesn't actually mean 32-\/bit, so we have to avoid STBI\_\_X64\_TARGET}}
\DoxyCodeLine{708 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{709 \textcolor{comment}{// 32-\/bit MinGW wants ESP to be 16-\/byte aligned, but this is not in the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{710 \textcolor{comment}{// Windows ABI and VC++ as well as Windows DLLs don't maintain that invariant.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{711 \textcolor{comment}{// As a result, enabling SSE2 on 32-\/bit MinGW is dangerous when not}}
\DoxyCodeLine{712 \textcolor{comment}{// simultaneously enabling "{}-\/mstackrealign"{}.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{713 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{714 \textcolor{comment}{// See https://github.com/nothings/stb/issues/81 for more information.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{715 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{716 \textcolor{comment}{// So default to no SSE2 on 32-\/bit MinGW. If you've read this far and added}}
\DoxyCodeLine{717 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/mstackrealign to your build settings, feel free to \#define STBI\_MINGW\_ENABLE\_SSE2.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{718 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define STBI\_NO\_SIMD}}
\DoxyCodeLine{719 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{720 }
\DoxyCodeLine{721 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#if !defined(STBI\_NO\_SIMD) \&\& (defined(STBI\_\_X86\_TARGET) || defined(STBI\_\_X64\_TARGET))}}

\DoxyCodeLine{986 }
\DoxyCodeLine{987 \textcolor{comment}{// stb\_image uses ints pervasively, including for offset calculations.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{988 \textcolor{comment}{// therefore the largest decoded image size we can support with the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{989 \textcolor{comment}{// current code, even on 64-\/bit targets, is INT\_MAX. this is not a}}
\DoxyCodeLine{990 \textcolor{comment}{// significant limitation for the intended use case.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{991 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{992 \textcolor{comment}{// we do, however, need to make sure our size calculations don't}}
\DoxyCodeLine{993 \textcolor{comment}{// overflow. hence a few helper functions for size calculations that}}
\DoxyCodeLine{994 \textcolor{comment}{// multiply integers together, making sure that they're non-\/negative}}
\DoxyCodeLine{995 \textcolor{comment}{// and no overflow occurs.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{996 }
\DoxyCodeLine{997 \textcolor{comment}{// return 1 if the sum is valid, 0 on overflow.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{998 \textcolor{comment}{// negative terms are considered invalid.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{999 \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} stbi\_\_addsizes\_valid(\textcolor{keywordtype}{int} a, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} b)}
\DoxyCodeLine{1000 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1001    \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (b < 0) \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1002    \textcolor{comment}{// now 0 <= b <= INT\_MAX, hence also}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1003    \textcolor{comment}{// 0 <= INT\_MAX -\/ b <= INTMAX.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1004    \textcolor{comment}{// And "{}a + b <= INT\_MAX"{} (which might overflow) is the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1005    \textcolor{comment}{// same as a <= INT\_MAX -\/ b (no overflow)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1006    \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} a <= INT\_MAX -\/ b;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1007 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1008 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1009 \textcolor{comment}{// returns 1 if the product is valid, 0 on overflow.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1010 \textcolor{comment}{// negative factors are considered invalid.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1011 \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} stbi\_\_mul2sizes\_valid(\textcolor{keywordtype}{int} a, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} b)}
\DoxyCodeLine{1012 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1013    \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (a < 0 || b < 0) \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1014    \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (b == 0) \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} 1; \textcolor{comment}{// mul-\/by-\/0 is always safe}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1015    \textcolor{comment}{// portable way to check for no overflows in a*b}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1016    \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} a <= INT\_MAX/b;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1017 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1018 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1019 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#if !defined(STBI\_NO\_JPEG) || !defined(STBI\_NO\_PNG) || !defined(STBI\_NO\_TGA) || !defined(STBI\_NO\_HDR)}}

\DoxyCodeLine{1893 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1894 \textcolor{comment}{//  "{}baseline"{} JPEG/JFIF decoder}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1895 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1896 \textcolor{comment}{//    simple implementation}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1897 \textcolor{comment}{//      -\/ doesn't support delayed output of y-\/dimension}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1898 \textcolor{comment}{//      -\/ simple interface (only one output format: 8-\/bit interleaved RGB)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1899 \textcolor{comment}{//      -\/ doesn't try to recover corrupt jpegs}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1900 \textcolor{comment}{//      -\/ doesn't allow partial loading, loading multiple at once}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1901 \textcolor{comment}{//      -\/ still fast on x86 (copying globals into locals doesn't help x86)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1902 \textcolor{comment}{//      -\/ allocates lots of intermediate memory (full size of all components)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1903 \textcolor{comment}{//        -\/ non-\/interleaved case requires this anyway}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1904 \textcolor{comment}{//        -\/ allows good upsampling (see next)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1905 \textcolor{comment}{//    high-\/quality}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1906 \textcolor{comment}{//      -\/ upsampled channels are bilinearly interpolated, even across blocks}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1907 \textcolor{comment}{//      -\/ quality integer IDCT derived from IJG's 'slow'}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1908 \textcolor{comment}{//    performance}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1909 \textcolor{comment}{//      -\/ fast huffman; reasonable integer IDCT}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1910 \textcolor{comment}{//      -\/ some SIMD kernels for common paths on targets with SSE2/NEON}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1911 \textcolor{comment}{//      -\/ uses a lot of intermediate memory, could cache poorly}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1912 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1913 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#ifndef STBI\_NO\_JPEG}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1914 }

\DoxyCodeLine{1983 \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} stbi\_\_build\_huffman(stbi\_\_huffman *h, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} *count)}

\DoxyCodeLine{1987    \textcolor{comment}{// build size list for each symbol (from JPEG spec)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1988    \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (i=0; i < 16; ++i)}
\DoxyCodeLine{1989       \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (j=0; j < count[i]; ++j)}
\DoxyCodeLine{1990          h-\/>size[k++] = (stbi\_uc) (i+1);}
\DoxyCodeLine{1991    h-\/>size[k] = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1992 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1993    \textcolor{comment}{// compute actual symbols (from jpeg spec)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1994    code = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1995    k = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1996    \textcolor{keywordflow}{for}(j=1; j <= 16; ++j) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1997       \textcolor{comment}{// compute delta to add to code to compute symbol id}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1998       h-\/>delta[j] = k -\/ code;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1999       \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (h-\/>size[k] == j) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2000          \textcolor{keywordflow}{while} (h-\/>size[k] == j)}
\DoxyCodeLine{2001             h-\/>code[k++] = (stbi\_\_uint16) (code++);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2002          \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (code-\/1 >= (1u << j)) \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} stbi\_\_err(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}bad code lengths"{}},\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}Corrupt JPEG"{}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{2003       \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2004       \textcolor{comment}{// compute largest code + 1 for this size, preshifted as needed later}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2005       h-\/>maxcode[j] = code << (16-\/j);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2006       code <<= 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2007    \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2008    h-\/>maxcode[j] = 0xffffffff;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2009 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2010    \textcolor{comment}{// build non-\/spec acceleration table; 255 is flag for not-\/accelerated}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2011    memset(h-\/>fast, 255, 1 << FAST\_BITS);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2012    \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (i=0; i < k; ++i) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2013       \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} s = h-\/>size[i];}
\DoxyCodeLine{2014       \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (s <= FAST\_BITS) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2015          \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} c = h-\/>code[i] << (FAST\_BITS-\/s);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2016          \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} m = 1 << (FAST\_BITS-\/s);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2017          \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (j=0; j < m; ++j) \{}

\DoxyCodeLine{2019          \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2020       \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2021    \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2022    \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} 1;}

\DoxyCodeLine{2025 \textcolor{comment}{// build a table that decodes both magnitude and value of small ACs in}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2026 \textcolor{comment}{// one go.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2027 \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} stbi\_\_build\_fast\_ac(stbi\_\_int16 *fast\_ac, stbi\_\_huffman *h)}
\DoxyCodeLine{2028 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2029    \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} i;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2030    \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (i=0; i < (1 << FAST\_BITS); ++i) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2031       stbi\_uc fast = h-\/>fast[i];}
\DoxyCodeLine{2032       fast\_ac[i] = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2033       \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (fast < 255) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2034          \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} rs = h-\/>values[fast];}
\DoxyCodeLine{2035          \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} run = (rs >> 4) \& 15;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2036          \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} magbits = rs \& 15;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2037          \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} len = h-\/>size[fast];}
\DoxyCodeLine{2038 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2039          \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (magbits \&\& len + magbits <= FAST\_BITS) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2040             \textcolor{comment}{// magnitude code followed by receive\_extend code}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2041             \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} k = ((i << len) \& ((1 << FAST\_BITS) -\/ 1)) >> (FAST\_BITS -\/ magbits);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2042             \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} m = 1 << (magbits -\/ 1);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2043             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (k < m) k += (\string~0U << magbits) + 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2044             \textcolor{comment}{// if the result is small enough, we can fit it in fast\_ac table}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2045             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (k >= -\/128 \&\& k <= 127)}
\DoxyCodeLine{2046                fast\_ac[i] = (stbi\_\_int16) ((k * 256) + (run * 16) + (len + magbits));}
\DoxyCodeLine{2047          \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2048       \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2049    \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2050 \}}

\DoxyCodeLine{2078 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2079    \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (j-\/>code\_bits < 16) stbi\_\_grow\_buffer\_unsafe(j);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2080 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2081    \textcolor{comment}{// look at the top FAST\_BITS and determine what symbol ID it is,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2082    \textcolor{comment}{// if the code is <= FAST\_BITS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2083    c = (j-\/>code\_buffer >> (32 -\/ FAST\_BITS)) \& ((1 << FAST\_BITS)-\/1);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2084    k = h-\/>fast[c];}

\DoxyCodeLine{2086       \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} s = h-\/>size[k];}
\DoxyCodeLine{2087       \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (s > j-\/>code\_bits)}
\DoxyCodeLine{2088          \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} -\/1;}

\DoxyCodeLine{2090       j-\/>code\_bits -\/= s;}

\DoxyCodeLine{2092    \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2093 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2094    \textcolor{comment}{// naive test is to shift the code\_buffer down so k bits are}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2095    \textcolor{comment}{// valid, then test against maxcode. To speed this up, we've}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2096    \textcolor{comment}{// preshifted maxcode left so that it has (16-\/k) 0s at the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2097    \textcolor{comment}{// end; in other words, regardless of the number of bits, it}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2098    \textcolor{comment}{// wants to be compared against something shifted to have 16;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2099    \textcolor{comment}{// that way we don't need to shift inside the loop.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2100    temp = j-\/>code\_buffer >> 16;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2101    \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (k=FAST\_BITS+1 ; ; ++k)}
\DoxyCodeLine{2102       \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (temp < h-\/>maxcode[k])}
\DoxyCodeLine{2103          \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{2104    \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (k == 17) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2105       \textcolor{comment}{// error! code not found}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2106       j-\/>code\_bits -\/= 16;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2107       \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} -\/1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2108    \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2109 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2110    \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (k > j-\/>code\_bits)}
\DoxyCodeLine{2111       \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} -\/1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2112 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2113    \textcolor{comment}{// convert the huffman code to the symbol id}}

\DoxyCodeLine{2115    STBI\_ASSERT((((j-\/>code\_buffer) >> (32 -\/ h-\/>size[c])) \& stbi\_\_bmask[h-\/>size[c]]) == h-\/>code[c]);}

\DoxyCodeLine{2117    \textcolor{comment}{// convert the id to a symbol}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2118    j-\/>code\_bits -\/= k;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2119    j-\/>code\_buffer <<= k;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2120    \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} h-\/>values[c];}

\DoxyCodeLine{2432 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2433 \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} stbi\_\_idct\_block(stbi\_uc *out, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} out\_stride, \textcolor{keywordtype}{short} data[64])}
\DoxyCodeLine{2434 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2435    \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} i,val[64],*v=val;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2436    stbi\_uc *o;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2437    \textcolor{keywordtype}{short} *d = data;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2438 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2439    \textcolor{comment}{// columns}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2440    \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (i=0; i < 8; ++i,++d, ++v) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2441       \textcolor{comment}{// if all zeroes, shortcut -\/-\/ this avoids dequantizing 0s and IDCTing}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2442       \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (d[ 8]==0 \&\& d[16]==0 \&\& d[24]==0 \&\& d[32]==0}
\DoxyCodeLine{2443            \&\& d[40]==0 \&\& d[48]==0 \&\& d[56]==0) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2444          \textcolor{comment}{//    no shortcut                 0     seconds}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2445          \textcolor{comment}{//    (1|2|3|4|5|6|7)==0          0     seconds}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2446          \textcolor{comment}{//    all separate               -\/0.047 seconds}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2447          \textcolor{comment}{//    1 \&\& 2|3 \&\& 4|5 \&\& 6|7:    -\/0.047 seconds}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2448          \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} dcterm = d[0]*4;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2449          v[0] = v[8] = v[16] = v[24] = v[32] = v[40] = v[48] = v[56] = dcterm;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2450       \} \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2451          STBI\_\_IDCT\_1D(d[ 0],d[ 8],d[16],d[24],d[32],d[40],d[48],d[56])}
\DoxyCodeLine{2452          \textcolor{comment}{// constants scaled things up by 1<<12; let's bring them back}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2453          \textcolor{comment}{// down, but keep 2 extra bits of precision}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2454          x0 += 512; x1 += 512; x2 += 512; x3 += 512;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2455          v[ 0] = (x0+t3) >> 10;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2456          v[56] = (x0-\/t3) >> 10;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2457          v[ 8] = (x1+t2) >> 10;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2458          v[48] = (x1-\/t2) >> 10;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2459          v[16] = (x2+t1) >> 10;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2460          v[40] = (x2-\/t1) >> 10;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2461          v[24] = (x3+t0) >> 10;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2462          v[32] = (x3-\/t0) >> 10;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2463       \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2464    \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2465 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2466    \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (i=0, v=val, o=out; i < 8; ++i,v+=8,o+=out\_stride) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2467       \textcolor{comment}{// no fast case since the first 1D IDCT spread components out}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2468       STBI\_\_IDCT\_1D(v[0],v[1],v[2],v[3],v[4],v[5],v[6],v[7])}
\DoxyCodeLine{2469       \textcolor{comment}{// constants scaled things up by 1<<12, plus we had 1<<2 from first}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2470       \textcolor{comment}{// loop, plus horizontal and vertical each scale by sqrt(8) so together}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2471       \textcolor{comment}{// we've got an extra 1<<3, so 1<<17 total we need to remove.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2472       \textcolor{comment}{// so we want to round that, which means adding 0.5 * 1<<17,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2473       \textcolor{comment}{// aka 65536. Also, we'll end up with -\/128 to 127 that we want}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2474       \textcolor{comment}{// to encode as 0..255 by adding 128, so we'll add that before the shift}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2475       x0 += 65536 + (128<<17);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2476       x1 += 65536 + (128<<17);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2477       x2 += 65536 + (128<<17);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2478       x3 += 65536 + (128<<17);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2479       \textcolor{comment}{// tried computing the shifts into temps, or'ing the temps to see}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2480       \textcolor{comment}{// if any were out of range, but that was slower}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2481       o[0] = stbi\_\_clamp((x0+t3) >> 17);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2482       o[7] = stbi\_\_clamp((x0-\/t3) >> 17);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2483       o[1] = stbi\_\_clamp((x1+t2) >> 17);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2484       o[6] = stbi\_\_clamp((x1-\/t2) >> 17);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2485       o[2] = stbi\_\_clamp((x2+t1) >> 17);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2486       o[5] = stbi\_\_clamp((x2-\/t1) >> 17);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2487       o[3] = stbi\_\_clamp((x3+t0) >> 17);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2488       o[4] = stbi\_\_clamp((x3-\/t0) >> 17);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2489    \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2490 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2491 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2492 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#ifdef STBI\_SSE2}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2493 \textcolor{comment}{// sse2 integer IDCT. not the fastest possible implementation but it}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2494 \textcolor{comment}{// produces bit-\/identical results to the generic C version so it's}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2495 \textcolor{comment}{// fully "{}transparent"{}.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2496 \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} stbi\_\_idct\_simd(stbi\_uc *out, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} out\_stride, \textcolor{keywordtype}{short} data[64])}
\DoxyCodeLine{2497 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2498    \textcolor{comment}{// This is constructed to match our regular (generic) integer IDCT exactly.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2499    \_\_m128i row0, row1, row2, row3, row4, row5, row6, row7;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2500    \_\_m128i tmp;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2501 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2502    \textcolor{comment}{// dot product constant: even elems=x, odd elems=y}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2503 \textcolor{preprocessor}{   \#define dct\_const(x,y)  \_mm\_setr\_epi16((x),(y),(x),(y),(x),(y),(x),(y))}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2504 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2505    \textcolor{comment}{// out(0) = c0[even]*x + c0[odd]*y   (c0, x, y 16-\/bit, out 32-\/bit)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2506    \textcolor{comment}{// out(1) = c1[even]*x + c1[odd]*y}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2507 \textcolor{preprocessor}{   \#define dct\_rot(out0,out1, x,y,c0,c1) \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2508 \textcolor{preprocessor}{      \_\_m128i c0\#\#lo = \_mm\_unpacklo\_epi16((x),(y)); \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2509 \textcolor{preprocessor}{      \_\_m128i c0\#\#hi = \_mm\_unpackhi\_epi16((x),(y)); \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2510 \textcolor{preprocessor}{      \_\_m128i out0\#\#\_l = \_mm\_madd\_epi16(c0\#\#lo, c0); \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2511 \textcolor{preprocessor}{      \_\_m128i out0\#\#\_h = \_mm\_madd\_epi16(c0\#\#hi, c0); \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2512 \textcolor{preprocessor}{      \_\_m128i out1\#\#\_l = \_mm\_madd\_epi16(c0\#\#lo, c1); \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2513 \textcolor{preprocessor}{      \_\_m128i out1\#\#\_h = \_mm\_madd\_epi16(c0\#\#hi, c1)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2514 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2515    \textcolor{comment}{// out = in << 12  (in 16-\/bit, out 32-\/bit)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2516 \textcolor{preprocessor}{   \#define dct\_widen(out, in) \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2517 \textcolor{preprocessor}{      \_\_m128i out\#\#\_l = \_mm\_srai\_epi32(\_mm\_unpacklo\_epi16(\_mm\_setzero\_si128(), (in)), 4); \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2518 \textcolor{preprocessor}{      \_\_m128i out\#\#\_h = \_mm\_srai\_epi32(\_mm\_unpackhi\_epi16(\_mm\_setzero\_si128(), (in)), 4)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2519 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2520    \textcolor{comment}{// wide add}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2521 \textcolor{preprocessor}{   \#define dct\_wadd(out, a, b) \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2522 \textcolor{preprocessor}{      \_\_m128i out\#\#\_l = \_mm\_add\_epi32(a\#\#\_l, b\#\#\_l); \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2523 \textcolor{preprocessor}{      \_\_m128i out\#\#\_h = \_mm\_add\_epi32(a\#\#\_h, b\#\#\_h)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2524 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2525    \textcolor{comment}{// wide sub}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2526 \textcolor{preprocessor}{   \#define dct\_wsub(out, a, b) \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2527 \textcolor{preprocessor}{      \_\_m128i out\#\#\_l = \_mm\_sub\_epi32(a\#\#\_l, b\#\#\_l); \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2528 \textcolor{preprocessor}{      \_\_m128i out\#\#\_h = \_mm\_sub\_epi32(a\#\#\_h, b\#\#\_h)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2529 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2530    \textcolor{comment}{// butterfly a/b, add bias, then shift by "{}s"{} and pack}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2531 \textcolor{preprocessor}{   \#define dct\_bfly32o(out0, out1, a,b,bias,s) \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2532 \textcolor{preprocessor}{      \{ \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2533 \textcolor{preprocessor}{         \_\_m128i abiased\_l = \_mm\_add\_epi32(a\#\#\_l, bias); \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2534 \textcolor{preprocessor}{         \_\_m128i abiased\_h = \_mm\_add\_epi32(a\#\#\_h, bias); \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2535 \textcolor{preprocessor}{         dct\_wadd(sum, abiased, b); \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2536 \textcolor{preprocessor}{         dct\_wsub(dif, abiased, b); \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2537 \textcolor{preprocessor}{         out0 = \_mm\_packs\_epi32(\_mm\_srai\_epi32(sum\_l, s), \_mm\_srai\_epi32(sum\_h, s)); \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2538 \textcolor{preprocessor}{         out1 = \_mm\_packs\_epi32(\_mm\_srai\_epi32(dif\_l, s), \_mm\_srai\_epi32(dif\_h, s)); \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2539 \textcolor{preprocessor}{      \}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2540 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2541    \textcolor{comment}{// 8-\/bit interleave step (for transposes)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2542 \textcolor{preprocessor}{   \#define dct\_interleave8(a, b) \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2543 \textcolor{preprocessor}{      tmp = a; \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2544 \textcolor{preprocessor}{      a = \_mm\_unpacklo\_epi8(a, b); \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2545 \textcolor{preprocessor}{      b = \_mm\_unpackhi\_epi8(tmp, b)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2546 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2547    \textcolor{comment}{// 16-\/bit interleave step (for transposes)}}

\DoxyCodeLine{2549 \textcolor{preprocessor}{      tmp = a; \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2550 \textcolor{preprocessor}{      a = \_mm\_unpacklo\_epi16(a, b); \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2551 \textcolor{preprocessor}{      b = \_mm\_unpackhi\_epi16(tmp, b)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2552 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2553 \textcolor{preprocessor}{   \#define dct\_pass(bias,shift) \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2554 \textcolor{preprocessor}{      \{ \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2555 \textcolor{preprocessor}{         }\textcolor{comment}{/* even part */}\textcolor{preprocessor}{ \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2556 \textcolor{preprocessor}{         dct\_rot(t2e,t3e, row2,row6, rot0\_0,rot0\_1); \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2557 \textcolor{preprocessor}{         \_\_m128i sum04 = \_mm\_add\_epi16(row0, row4); \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2558 \textcolor{preprocessor}{         \_\_m128i dif04 = \_mm\_sub\_epi16(row0, row4); \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2559 \textcolor{preprocessor}{         dct\_widen(t0e, sum04); \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2560 \textcolor{preprocessor}{         dct\_widen(t1e, dif04); \(\backslash\)}}

\DoxyCodeLine{2566 \textcolor{preprocessor}{         dct\_rot(y0o,y2o, row7,row3, rot2\_0,rot2\_1); \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2567 \textcolor{preprocessor}{         dct\_rot(y1o,y3o, row5,row1, rot3\_0,rot3\_1); \(\backslash\)}}

\DoxyCodeLine{2569 \textcolor{preprocessor}{         \_\_m128i sum35 = \_mm\_add\_epi16(row3, row5); \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2570 \textcolor{preprocessor}{         dct\_rot(y4o,y5o, sum17,sum35, rot1\_0,rot1\_1); \(\backslash\)}}

\DoxyCodeLine{2576 \textcolor{preprocessor}{         dct\_bfly32o(row1,row6, x1,x6,bias,shift); \(\backslash\)}}

\DoxyCodeLine{2578 \textcolor{preprocessor}{         dct\_bfly32o(row3,row4, x3,x4,bias,shift); \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2579 \textcolor{preprocessor}{      \}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2580 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2581    \_\_m128i rot0\_0 = dct\_const(stbi\_\_f2f(0.5411961f), stbi\_\_f2f(0.5411961f) + stbi\_\_f2f(-\/1.847759065f));}

\DoxyCodeLine{2590    \textcolor{comment}{// rounding biases in column/row passes, see stbi\_\_idct\_block for explanation.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{2632       \_\_m128i p0 = \_mm\_packus\_epi16(row0, row1); \textcolor{comment}{// a0a1a2a3...a7b0b1b2b3...b7}}

\DoxyCodeLine{2649       \textcolor{comment}{// store}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2650       \_mm\_storel\_epi64((\_\_m128i *) out, p0); out += out\_stride;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2651       \_mm\_storel\_epi64((\_\_m128i *) out, \_mm\_shuffle\_epi32(p0, 0x4e)); out += out\_stride;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2652       \_mm\_storel\_epi64((\_\_m128i *) out, p2); out += out\_stride;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2653       \_mm\_storel\_epi64((\_\_m128i *) out, \_mm\_shuffle\_epi32(p2, 0x4e)); out += out\_stride;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2654       \_mm\_storel\_epi64((\_\_m128i *) out, p1); out += out\_stride;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2655       \_mm\_storel\_epi64((\_\_m128i *) out, \_mm\_shuffle\_epi32(p1, 0x4e)); out += out\_stride;}

\DoxyCodeLine{2657       \_mm\_storel\_epi64((\_\_m128i *) out, \_mm\_shuffle\_epi32(p3, 0x4e));}
\DoxyCodeLine{2658    \}}

\DoxyCodeLine{2881 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define STBI\_\_MARKER\_none  0xff}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2882 \textcolor{comment}{// if there's a pending marker from the entropy stream, return that}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2883 \textcolor{comment}{// otherwise, fetch from the stream and get a marker. if there's no}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2884 \textcolor{comment}{// marker, return 0xff, which is never a valid marker value}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2885 \textcolor{keyword}{static} stbi\_uc stbi\_\_get\_marker(stbi\_\_jpeg *j)}
\DoxyCodeLine{2886 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2887    stbi\_uc x;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2888    \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (j-\/>marker != STBI\_\_MARKER\_none) \{ x = j-\/>marker; j-\/>marker = STBI\_\_MARKER\_none; \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} x; \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2889    x = stbi\_\_get8(j-\/>s);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2890    \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (x != 0xff) \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} STBI\_\_MARKER\_none;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2891    \textcolor{keywordflow}{while} (x == 0xff)}
\DoxyCodeLine{2892       x = stbi\_\_get8(j-\/>s); \textcolor{comment}{// consume repeated 0xff fill bytes}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2893    \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} x;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2894 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2895 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2896 \textcolor{comment}{// in each scan, we'll have scan\_n components, and the order}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2897 \textcolor{comment}{// of the components is specified by order[]}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2898 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define STBI\_\_RESTART(x)     ((x) >= 0xd0 \&\& (x) <= 0xd7)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2899 }

\DoxyCodeLine{3491 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#if defined(STBI\_SSE2)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3492       \textcolor{comment}{// load and perform the vertical filtering pass}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3493       \textcolor{comment}{// this uses 3*x + y = 4*x + (y -\/ x)}}

\DoxyCodeLine{3497       \_\_m128i farw  = \_mm\_unpacklo\_epi8(farb, zero);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3498       \_\_m128i nearw = \_mm\_unpacklo\_epi8(nearb, zero);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3499       \_\_m128i diff  = \_mm\_sub\_epi16(farw, nearw);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3500       \_\_m128i nears = \_mm\_slli\_epi16(nearw, 2);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3501       \_\_m128i curr  = \_mm\_add\_epi16(nears, diff); \textcolor{comment}{// current row}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3502 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3503       \textcolor{comment}{// horizontal filter works the same based on shifted vers of current}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3504       \textcolor{comment}{// row. "{}prev"{} is current row shifted right by 1 pixel; we need to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3505       \textcolor{comment}{// insert the previous pixel value (from t1).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3506       \textcolor{comment}{// "{}next"{} is current row shifted left by 1 pixel, with first pixel}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3507       \textcolor{comment}{// of next block of 8 pixels added in.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3508       \_\_m128i prv0 = \_mm\_slli\_si128(curr, 2);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3509       \_\_m128i nxt0 = \_mm\_srli\_si128(curr, 2);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3510       \_\_m128i prev = \_mm\_insert\_epi16(prv0, t1, 0);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3511       \_\_m128i next = \_mm\_insert\_epi16(nxt0, 3*in\_near[i+8] + in\_far[i+8], 7);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3512 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3513       \textcolor{comment}{// horizontal filter, polyphase implementation since it's convenient:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3514       \textcolor{comment}{// even pixels = 3*cur + prev = cur*4 + (prev -\/ cur)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3515       \textcolor{comment}{// odd  pixels = 3*cur + next = cur*4 + (next -\/ cur)}}

\DoxyCodeLine{3521       \_\_m128i curb = \_mm\_add\_epi16(curs, bias);}

\DoxyCodeLine{3523       \_\_m128i odd  = \_mm\_add\_epi16(nxtd, curb);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3524 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3525       \textcolor{comment}{// interleave even and odd pixels, then undo scaling.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{3542 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3543       \textcolor{comment}{// horizontal filter works the same based on shifted vers of current}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3544       \textcolor{comment}{// row. "{}prev"{} is current row shifted right by 1 pixel; we need to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3545       \textcolor{comment}{// insert the previous pixel value (from t1).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3546       \textcolor{comment}{// "{}next"{} is current row shifted left by 1 pixel, with first pixel}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3547       \textcolor{comment}{// of next block of 8 pixels added in.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3548       int16x8\_t prv0 = vextq\_s16(curr, curr, 7);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3549       int16x8\_t nxt0 = vextq\_s16(curr, curr, 1);}

\DoxyCodeLine{3556       \textcolor{comment}{// note the shared term.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3557       int16x8\_t curs = vshlq\_n\_s16(curr, 2);}

\DoxyCodeLine{3565       o.val[0] = vqrshrun\_n\_s16(even, 4);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3566       o.val[1] = vqrshrun\_n\_s16(odd,  4);}

\DoxyCodeLine{3592 \textcolor{keyword}{static} stbi\_uc *stbi\_\_resample\_row\_generic(stbi\_uc *out, stbi\_uc *in\_near, stbi\_uc *in\_far, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} w, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} hs)}

\DoxyCodeLine{3601 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3602 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3603 \textcolor{comment}{// this is a reduced-\/precision calculation of YCbCr-\/to-\/RGB introduced}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3604 \textcolor{comment}{// to make sure the code produces the same results in both SIMD and scalar}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3605 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define stbi\_\_float2fixed(x)  (((int) ((x) * 4096.0f + 0.5f)) << 8)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3606 \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} stbi\_\_YCbCr\_to\_RGB\_row(stbi\_uc *out, \textcolor{keyword}{const} stbi\_uc *y, \textcolor{keyword}{const} stbi\_uc *pcb, \textcolor{keyword}{const} stbi\_uc *pcr, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} count, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} step)}
\DoxyCodeLine{3607 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3608    \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} i;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3609    \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (i=0; i < count; ++i) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3610       \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} y\_fixed = (y[i] << 20) + (1<<19); \textcolor{comment}{// rounding}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3611       \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} r,g,b;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3612       \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} cr = pcr[i] -\/ 128;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3613       \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} cb = pcb[i] -\/ 128;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3614       r = y\_fixed +  cr* stbi\_\_float2fixed(1.40200f);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3615       g = y\_fixed + (cr*-\/stbi\_\_float2fixed(0.71414f)) + ((cb*-\/stbi\_\_float2fixed(0.34414f)) \& 0xffff0000);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3616       b = y\_fixed                                     +   cb* stbi\_\_float2fixed(1.77200f);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3617       r >>= 20;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3618       g >>= 20;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3619       b >>= 20;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3620       \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} ((\textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned}) r > 255) \{ \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (r < 0) r = 0; \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} r = 255; \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3621       \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} ((\textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned}) g > 255) \{ \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (g < 0) g = 0; \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} g = 255; \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3622       \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} ((\textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned}) b > 255) \{ \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (b < 0) b = 0; \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} b = 255; \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3623       out[0] = (stbi\_uc)r;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3624       out[1] = (stbi\_uc)g;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3625       out[2] = (stbi\_uc)b;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3626       out[3] = 255;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3627       out += \mbox{\hyperlink{group__core__func__common_ga015a1261ff23e12650211aa872863cce}{step}};}
\DoxyCodeLine{3628    \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3629 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3630 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3631 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#if defined(STBI\_SSE2) || defined(STBI\_NEON)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3632 \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} stbi\_\_YCbCr\_to\_RGB\_simd(stbi\_uc *out, stbi\_uc \textcolor{keyword}{const} *y, stbi\_uc \textcolor{keyword}{const} *pcb, stbi\_uc \textcolor{keyword}{const} *pcr, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} count, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} step)}
\DoxyCodeLine{3633 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3634    \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} i = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3635 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3636 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#ifdef STBI\_SSE2}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3637    \textcolor{comment}{// step == 3 is pretty ugly on the final interleave, and i'm not convinced}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3638    \textcolor{comment}{// it's useful in practice (you wouldn't use it for textures, for example).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3639    \textcolor{comment}{// so just accelerate step == 4 case.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3640    \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (step == 4) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3641       \textcolor{comment}{// this is a fairly straightforward implementation and not super-\/optimized.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3642       \_\_m128i signflip  = \_mm\_set1\_epi8(-\/0x80);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3643       \_\_m128i cr\_const0 = \_mm\_set1\_epi16(   (\textcolor{keywordtype}{short}) ( 1.40200f*4096.0f+0.5f));}
\DoxyCodeLine{3644       \_\_m128i cr\_const1 = \_mm\_set1\_epi16( -\/ (\textcolor{keywordtype}{short}) ( 0.71414f*4096.0f+0.5f));}
\DoxyCodeLine{3645       \_\_m128i cb\_const0 = \_mm\_set1\_epi16( -\/ (\textcolor{keywordtype}{short}) ( 0.34414f*4096.0f+0.5f));}
\DoxyCodeLine{3646       \_\_m128i cb\_const1 = \_mm\_set1\_epi16(   (\textcolor{keywordtype}{short}) ( 1.77200f*4096.0f+0.5f));}
\DoxyCodeLine{3647       \_\_m128i y\_bias = \_mm\_set1\_epi8((\textcolor{keywordtype}{char}) (\textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char}) 128);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3648       \_\_m128i xw = \_mm\_set1\_epi16(255); \textcolor{comment}{// alpha channel}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3649 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3650       \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (; i+7 < count; i += 8) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3651          \textcolor{comment}{// load}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3652          \_\_m128i y\_bytes = \_mm\_loadl\_epi64((\_\_m128i *) (y+i));}
\DoxyCodeLine{3653          \_\_m128i cr\_bytes = \_mm\_loadl\_epi64((\_\_m128i *) (pcr+i));}
\DoxyCodeLine{3654          \_\_m128i cb\_bytes = \_mm\_loadl\_epi64((\_\_m128i *) (pcb+i));}
\DoxyCodeLine{3655          \_\_m128i cr\_biased = \_mm\_xor\_si128(cr\_bytes, signflip); \textcolor{comment}{// -\/128}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3656          \_\_m128i cb\_biased = \_mm\_xor\_si128(cb\_bytes, signflip); \textcolor{comment}{// -\/128}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3657 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3658          \textcolor{comment}{// unpack to short (and left-\/shift cr, cb by 8)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3659          \_\_m128i yw  = \_mm\_unpacklo\_epi8(y\_bias, y\_bytes);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3660          \_\_m128i crw = \_mm\_unpacklo\_epi8(\_mm\_setzero\_si128(), cr\_biased);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3661          \_\_m128i cbw = \_mm\_unpacklo\_epi8(\_mm\_setzero\_si128(), cb\_biased);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3662 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3663          \textcolor{comment}{// color transform}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3664          \_\_m128i yws = \_mm\_srli\_epi16(yw, 4);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3665          \_\_m128i cr0 = \_mm\_mulhi\_epi16(cr\_const0, crw);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3666          \_\_m128i cb0 = \_mm\_mulhi\_epi16(cb\_const0, cbw);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3667          \_\_m128i cb1 = \_mm\_mulhi\_epi16(cbw, cb\_const1);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3668          \_\_m128i cr1 = \_mm\_mulhi\_epi16(crw, cr\_const1);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3669          \_\_m128i rws = \_mm\_add\_epi16(cr0, yws);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3670          \_\_m128i gwt = \_mm\_add\_epi16(cb0, yws);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3671          \_\_m128i bws = \_mm\_add\_epi16(yws, cb1);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3672          \_\_m128i gws = \_mm\_add\_epi16(gwt, cr1);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3673 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3674          \textcolor{comment}{// descale}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3675          \_\_m128i rw = \_mm\_srai\_epi16(rws, 4);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3676          \_\_m128i bw = \_mm\_srai\_epi16(bws, 4);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3677          \_\_m128i gw = \_mm\_srai\_epi16(gws, 4);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3678 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3679          \textcolor{comment}{// back to byte, set up for transpose}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3680          \_\_m128i brb = \_mm\_packus\_epi16(rw, bw);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3681          \_\_m128i gxb = \_mm\_packus\_epi16(gw, xw);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3682 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3683          \textcolor{comment}{// transpose to interleave channels}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3684          \_\_m128i t0 = \_mm\_unpacklo\_epi8(brb, gxb);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3685          \_\_m128i t1 = \_mm\_unpackhi\_epi8(brb, gxb);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3686          \_\_m128i o0 = \_mm\_unpacklo\_epi16(t0, t1);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3687          \_\_m128i o1 = \_mm\_unpackhi\_epi16(t0, t1);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3688 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3689          \textcolor{comment}{// store}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3690          \_mm\_storeu\_si128((\_\_m128i *) (out + 0), o0);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3691          \_mm\_storeu\_si128((\_\_m128i *) (out + 16), o1);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3692          out += 32;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3693       \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3694    \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3695 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3696 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3697 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#ifdef STBI\_NEON}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3698    \textcolor{comment}{// in this version, step=3 support would be easy to add. but is there demand?}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3699    \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (step == 4) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3700       \textcolor{comment}{// this is a fairly straightforward implementation and not super-\/optimized.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3701       uint8x8\_t signflip = vdup\_n\_u8(0x80);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3702       int16x8\_t cr\_const0 = vdupq\_n\_s16(   (\textcolor{keywordtype}{short}) ( 1.40200f*4096.0f+0.5f));}
\DoxyCodeLine{3703       int16x8\_t cr\_const1 = vdupq\_n\_s16( -\/ (\textcolor{keywordtype}{short}) ( 0.71414f*4096.0f+0.5f));}
\DoxyCodeLine{3704       int16x8\_t cb\_const0 = vdupq\_n\_s16( -\/ (\textcolor{keywordtype}{short}) ( 0.34414f*4096.0f+0.5f));}
\DoxyCodeLine{3705       int16x8\_t cb\_const1 = vdupq\_n\_s16(   (\textcolor{keywordtype}{short}) ( 1.77200f*4096.0f+0.5f));}
\DoxyCodeLine{3706 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3707       \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (; i+7 < count; i += 8) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3708          \textcolor{comment}{// load}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3709          uint8x8\_t y\_bytes  = vld1\_u8(y + i);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3710          uint8x8\_t cr\_bytes = vld1\_u8(pcr + i);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3711          uint8x8\_t cb\_bytes = vld1\_u8(pcb + i);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3712          int8x8\_t cr\_biased = vreinterpret\_s8\_u8(vsub\_u8(cr\_bytes, signflip));}
\DoxyCodeLine{3713          int8x8\_t cb\_biased = vreinterpret\_s8\_u8(vsub\_u8(cb\_bytes, signflip));}
\DoxyCodeLine{3714 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3715          \textcolor{comment}{// expand to s16}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3716          int16x8\_t yws = vreinterpretq\_s16\_u16(vshll\_n\_u8(y\_bytes, 4));}
\DoxyCodeLine{3717          int16x8\_t crw = vshll\_n\_s8(cr\_biased, 7);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3718          int16x8\_t cbw = vshll\_n\_s8(cb\_biased, 7);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3719 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3720          \textcolor{comment}{// color transform}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3721          int16x8\_t cr0 = vqdmulhq\_s16(crw, cr\_const0);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3722          int16x8\_t cb0 = vqdmulhq\_s16(cbw, cb\_const0);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3723          int16x8\_t cr1 = vqdmulhq\_s16(crw, cr\_const1);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3724          int16x8\_t cb1 = vqdmulhq\_s16(cbw, cb\_const1);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3725          int16x8\_t rws = vaddq\_s16(yws, cr0);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3726          int16x8\_t gws = vaddq\_s16(vaddq\_s16(yws, cb0), cr1);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3727          int16x8\_t bws = vaddq\_s16(yws, cb1);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3728 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3729          \textcolor{comment}{// undo scaling, round, convert to byte}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3730          uint8x8x4\_t o;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3731          o.val[0] = vqrshrun\_n\_s16(rws, 4);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3732          o.val[1] = vqrshrun\_n\_s16(gws, 4);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3733          o.val[2] = vqrshrun\_n\_s16(bws, 4);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3734          o.val[3] = vdup\_n\_u8(255);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3735 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3736          \textcolor{comment}{// store, interleaving r/g/b/a}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3737          vst4\_u8(out, o);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3738          out += 8*4;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3739       \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3740    \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3741 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3742 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3743    \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (; i < count; ++i) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3744       \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} y\_fixed = (y[i] << 20) + (1<<19); \textcolor{comment}{// rounding}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3745       \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} r,g,b;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3746       \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} cr = pcr[i] -\/ 128;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3747       \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} cb = pcb[i] -\/ 128;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3748       r = y\_fixed + cr* stbi\_\_float2fixed(1.40200f);}

\DoxyCodeLine{3750       b = y\_fixed                                   +   cb* stbi\_\_float2fixed(1.77200f);}

\DoxyCodeLine{3752       g >>= 20;}

\DoxyCodeLine{3756       \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} ((\textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned}) b > 255) \{ \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (b < 0) b = 0; \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} b = 255; \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3757       out[0] = (stbi\_uc)r;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3758       out[1] = (stbi\_uc)g;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3759       out[2] = (stbi\_uc)b;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3760       out[3] = 255;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3761       out += \mbox{\hyperlink{group__core__func__common_ga015a1261ff23e12650211aa872863cce}{step}};}

\DoxyCodeLine{4024 \textcolor{comment}{// public domain zlib decode    v0.2  Sean Barrett 2006-\/11-\/18}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4025 \textcolor{comment}{//    simple implementation}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4026 \textcolor{comment}{//      -\/ all input must be provided in an upfront buffer}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4027 \textcolor{comment}{//      -\/ all output is written to a single output buffer (can malloc/realloc)}}

\DoxyCodeLine{4029 \textcolor{comment}{//      -\/ fast huffman}}

\DoxyCodeLine{4032 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4033 \textcolor{comment}{// fast-\/way is faster to check than jpeg huffman, but slow way is slower}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4034 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define STBI\_\_ZFAST\_BITS  9 }\textcolor{comment}{// accelerate all cases in default tables}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4035 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define STBI\_\_ZFAST\_MASK  ((1 << STBI\_\_ZFAST\_BITS) -\/ 1)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4036 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define STBI\_\_ZNSYMS 288 }\textcolor{comment}{// number of symbols in literal/length alphabet}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4037 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4038 \textcolor{comment}{// zlib-\/style huffman encoding}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4039 \textcolor{comment}{// (jpegs packs from left, zlib from right, so can't share code)}}

\DoxyCodeLine{4050 stbi\_inline \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} stbi\_\_bitreverse16(\textcolor{keywordtype}{int} n)}
\DoxyCodeLine{4051 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4052   n = ((n \& 0xAAAA) >>  1) | ((n \& 0x5555) << 1);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4053   n = ((n \& 0xCCCC) >>  2) | ((n \& 0x3333) << 2);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4054   n = ((n \& 0xF0F0) >>  4) | ((n \& 0x0F0F) << 4);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4055   n = ((n \& 0xFF00) >>  8) | ((n \& 0x00FF) << 8);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4056   \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} n;}

\DoxyCodeLine{4518 \textcolor{comment}{// public domain "{}baseline"{} PNG decoder   v0.10  Sean Barrett 2006-\/11-\/18}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4519 \textcolor{comment}{//    simple implementation}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4520 \textcolor{comment}{//      -\/ only 8-\/bit samples}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4521 \textcolor{comment}{//      -\/ no CRC checking}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4522 \textcolor{comment}{//      -\/ allocates lots of intermediate memory}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4523 \textcolor{comment}{//        -\/ avoids problem of streaming data between subsystems}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4524 \textcolor{comment}{//        -\/ avoids explicit window management}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4525 \textcolor{comment}{//    performance}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4526 \textcolor{comment}{//      -\/ uses stb\_zlib, a PD zlib implementation with fast huffman decoding}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4527 }

\DoxyCodeLine{4642             \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} STBI\_\_F\_none       : cur[k] = raw[k]; \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{4643             \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} STBI\_\_F\_sub        : cur[k] = raw[k]; \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{4644             \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} STBI\_\_F\_up         : cur[k] = STBI\_\_BYTECAST(raw[k] + prior[k]); \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}

\DoxyCodeLine{4647             \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} STBI\_\_F\_avg\_first  : cur[k] = raw[k]; \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{4648             \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} STBI\_\_F\_paeth\_first: cur[k] = raw[k]; \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{4649          \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4650       \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4651 }

\DoxyCodeLine{4656          cur += out\_n;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4657          prior += out\_n;}

\DoxyCodeLine{4665          prior += output\_bytes;}

\DoxyCodeLine{4668          cur += 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4669          prior += 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4670       \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4671 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4672       \textcolor{comment}{// this is a little gross, so that we don't switch per-\/pixel or per-\/component}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4673       \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (depth < 8 || img\_n == out\_n) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4674          \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} nk = (width -\/ 1)*filter\_bytes;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4675 \textcolor{preprocessor}{         \#define STBI\_\_CASE(f) \(\backslash\)}}

\DoxyCodeLine{4677 \textcolor{preprocessor}{                for (k=0; k < nk; ++k)}}

\DoxyCodeLine{4679             \textcolor{comment}{// "{}none"{} filter turns into a memcpy here; make that explicit.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4680             \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} STBI\_\_F\_none:         memcpy(cur, raw, nk); \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}

\DoxyCodeLine{4707          \textcolor{comment}{// the loop above sets the high byte of the pixels' alpha, but for}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4708          \textcolor{comment}{// 16 bit png files we also need the low byte set. we'll do that here.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4709          \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (depth == 16) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4710             cur = a-\/>out + stride*j; \textcolor{comment}{// start at the beginning of the row again}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4711             \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (i=0; i < x; ++i,cur+=output\_bytes) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4712                cur[filter\_bytes+1] = 255;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4713             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4714          \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4715       \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4716    \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4717 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4718    \textcolor{comment}{// we make a separate pass to expand bits to pixels; for performance,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4719    \textcolor{comment}{// this could run two scanlines behind the above code, so it won't}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4720    \textcolor{comment}{// intefere with filtering but will still be in the cache.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4721    \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (depth < 8) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4722       \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (j=0; j < y; ++j) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4723          stbi\_uc *cur = a-\/>out + stride*j;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4724          stbi\_uc *in  = a-\/>out + stride*j + x*out\_n -\/ img\_width\_bytes;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4725          \textcolor{comment}{// unpack 1/2/4-\/bit into a 8-\/bit buffer. allows us to keep the common 8-\/bit path optimal at minimal cost for 1/2/4-\/bit}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4726          \textcolor{comment}{// png guarante byte alignment, if width is not multiple of 8/4/2 we'll decode dummy trailing data that will be skipped in the later loop}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4727          stbi\_uc \mbox{\hyperlink{group__ext__matrix__transform_gaae2f8b2080622b24b85e1096748599b6}{scale}} = (color == 0) ? stbi\_\_depth\_scale\_table[depth] : 1; \textcolor{comment}{// scale grayscale values to 0..255 range}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4728 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4729          \textcolor{comment}{// note that the final byte might overshoot and write more data than desired.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4730          \textcolor{comment}{// we can allocate enough data that this never writes out of memory, but it}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4731          \textcolor{comment}{// could also overwrite the next scanline. can it overwrite non-\/empty data}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4732          \textcolor{comment}{// on the next scanline? yes, consider 1-\/pixel-\/wide scanlines with 1-\/bit-\/per-\/pixel.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4733          \textcolor{comment}{// so we need to explicitly clamp the final ones}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4734 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4735          \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (depth == 4) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4736             \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (k=x*img\_n; k >= 2; k-\/=2, ++in) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4737                *cur++ = \mbox{\hyperlink{group__ext__matrix__transform_gaae2f8b2080622b24b85e1096748599b6}{scale}} * ((*in >> 4)       );}
\DoxyCodeLine{4738                *cur++ = \mbox{\hyperlink{group__ext__matrix__transform_gaae2f8b2080622b24b85e1096748599b6}{scale}} * ((*in     ) \& 0x0f);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4739             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4740             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (k > 0) *cur++ = \mbox{\hyperlink{group__ext__matrix__transform_gaae2f8b2080622b24b85e1096748599b6}{scale}} * ((*in >> 4)       );}
\DoxyCodeLine{4741          \} \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (depth == 2) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4742             \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (k=x*img\_n; k >= 4; k-\/=4, ++in) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4743                *cur++ = \mbox{\hyperlink{group__ext__matrix__transform_gaae2f8b2080622b24b85e1096748599b6}{scale}} * ((*in >> 6)       );}
\DoxyCodeLine{4744                *cur++ = \mbox{\hyperlink{group__ext__matrix__transform_gaae2f8b2080622b24b85e1096748599b6}{scale}} * ((*in >> 4) \& 0x03);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4745                *cur++ = \mbox{\hyperlink{group__ext__matrix__transform_gaae2f8b2080622b24b85e1096748599b6}{scale}} * ((*in >> 2) \& 0x03);}

\DoxyCodeLine{4749             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (k > 1) *cur++ = \mbox{\hyperlink{group__ext__matrix__transform_gaae2f8b2080622b24b85e1096748599b6}{scale}} * ((*in >> 4) \& 0x03);}

\DoxyCodeLine{4769          \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4770          \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (img\_n != out\_n) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4771             \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} q;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4772             \textcolor{comment}{// insert alpha = 255}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4773             cur = a-\/>out + stride*j;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4774             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (img\_n == 1) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4775                \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (q=x-\/1; q >= 0; -\/-\/q) \{}

\DoxyCodeLine{4777                   cur[q*2+0] = cur[q];}
\DoxyCodeLine{4778                \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4779             \} \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4780                STBI\_ASSERT(img\_n == 3);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4781                \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (q=x-\/1; q >= 0; -\/-\/q) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4782                   cur[q*4+3] = 255;}

\DoxyCodeLine{4784                   cur[q*4+1] = cur[q*3+1];}

\DoxyCodeLine{4786                \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4787             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4788          \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4789       \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4790    \} \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (depth == 16) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4791       \textcolor{comment}{// force the image data from big-\/endian to platform-\/native.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4792       \textcolor{comment}{// this is done in a separate pass due to the decoding relying}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4793       \textcolor{comment}{// on the data being untouched, but could probably be done}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4794       \textcolor{comment}{// per-\/line during decode if care is taken.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4795       stbi\_uc *cur = a-\/>out;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4796       stbi\_\_uint16 *cur16 = (stbi\_\_uint16*)cur;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4797 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4798       \textcolor{keywordflow}{for}(i=0; i < x*y*out\_n; ++i,cur16++,cur+=2) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4799          *cur16 = (cur[0] << 8) | cur[1];}
\DoxyCodeLine{4800       \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4801    \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4802 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4803    \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} 1;}

\DoxyCodeLine{4820       \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} yorig[] = \{ 0,0,4,0,2,0,1 \};}
\DoxyCodeLine{4821       \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} xspc[]  = \{ 8,8,4,4,2,2,1 \};}
\DoxyCodeLine{4822       \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} yspc[]  = \{ 8,8,8,4,4,2,2 \};}

\DoxyCodeLine{4824       \textcolor{comment}{// pass1\_x[4] = 0, pass1\_x[5] = 1, pass1\_x[12] = 1}}

\DoxyCodeLine{4826       y = (a-\/>s-\/>img\_y -\/ yorig[p] + yspc[p]-\/1) / yspc[p];}

\DoxyCodeLine{4831             \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4832          \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4833          \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (j=0; j < y; ++j) \{}

\DoxyCodeLine{5320    a = (a \& 0x55555555) + ((a >>  1) \& 0x55555555); \textcolor{comment}{// max 2}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5321    a = (a \& 0x33333333) + ((a >>  2) \& 0x33333333); \textcolor{comment}{// max 4}}
