\DoxyCodeLine{5742 \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} stbi\_\_tga\_test(stbi\_\_context *s)}
\DoxyCodeLine{5743 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5744    \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} res = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5745    \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} sz, tga\_color\_type;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5746    stbi\_\_get8(s);      \textcolor{comment}{//   discard Offset}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5747    tga\_color\_type = stbi\_\_get8(s);   \textcolor{comment}{//   color type}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5748    \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} ( tga\_color\_type > 1 ) \textcolor{keywordflow}{goto} errorEnd;   \textcolor{comment}{//   only RGB or indexed allowed}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5749    sz = stbi\_\_get8(s);   \textcolor{comment}{//   image type}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5750    \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} ( tga\_color\_type == 1 ) \{ \textcolor{comment}{// colormapped (paletted) image}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5751       \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (sz != 1 \&\& sz != 9) \textcolor{keywordflow}{goto} errorEnd; \textcolor{comment}{// colortype 1 demands image type 1 or 9}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5752       stbi\_\_skip(s,4);       \textcolor{comment}{// skip index of first colormap entry and number of entries}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5753       sz = stbi\_\_get8(s);    \textcolor{comment}{//   check bits per palette color entry}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5754       \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} ( (sz != 8) \&\& (sz != 15) \&\& (sz != 16) \&\& (sz != 24) \&\& (sz != 32) ) \textcolor{keywordflow}{goto} errorEnd;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5755       stbi\_\_skip(s,4);       \textcolor{comment}{// skip image x and y origin}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5756    \} \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \{ \textcolor{comment}{// "{}normal"{} image w/o colormap}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5757       \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} ( (sz != 2) \&\& (sz != 3) \&\& (sz != 10) \&\& (sz != 11) ) \textcolor{keywordflow}{goto} errorEnd; \textcolor{comment}{// only RGB or grey allowed, +/-\/ RLE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5758       stbi\_\_skip(s,9); \textcolor{comment}{// skip colormap specification and image x/y origin}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5759    \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5760    \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} ( stbi\_\_get16le(s) < 1 ) \textcolor{keywordflow}{goto} errorEnd;      \textcolor{comment}{//   test width}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5761    \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} ( stbi\_\_get16le(s) < 1 ) \textcolor{keywordflow}{goto} errorEnd;      \textcolor{comment}{//   test height}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5762    sz = stbi\_\_get8(s);   \textcolor{comment}{//   bits per pixel}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5763    \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} ( (tga\_color\_type == 1) \&\& (sz != 8) \&\& (sz != 16) ) \textcolor{keywordflow}{goto} errorEnd; \textcolor{comment}{// for colormapped images, bpp is size of an index}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5764    \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} ( (sz != 8) \&\& (sz != 15) \&\& (sz != 16) \&\& (sz != 24) \&\& (sz != 32) ) \textcolor{keywordflow}{goto} errorEnd;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5765 }
\DoxyCodeLine{5766    res = 1; \textcolor{comment}{// if we got this far, everything's good and we can return 1 instead of 0}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5767 }
\DoxyCodeLine{5768 errorEnd:}
\DoxyCodeLine{5769    stbi\_\_rewind(s);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5770    \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} res;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5771 \}}

\DoxyCodeLine{5773 \textcolor{comment}{// read 16bit value and convert to 24bit RGB}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5774 \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} stbi\_\_tga\_read\_rgb16(stbi\_\_context *s, stbi\_uc* out)}
\DoxyCodeLine{5775 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5776    stbi\_\_uint16 px = (stbi\_\_uint16)stbi\_\_get16le(s);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5777    stbi\_\_uint16 fiveBitMask = 31;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5778    \textcolor{comment}{// we have 3 channels with 5bits each}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5779    \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} r = (px >> 10) \& fiveBitMask;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5780    \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} g = (px >> 5) \& fiveBitMask;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5781    \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} b = px \& fiveBitMask;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5782    \textcolor{comment}{// Note that this saves the data in RGB(A) order, so it doesn't need to be swapped later}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5783    out[0] = (stbi\_uc)((r * 255)/31);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5784    out[1] = (stbi\_uc)((g * 255)/31);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5785    out[2] = (stbi\_uc)((b * 255)/31);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5786 }
\DoxyCodeLine{5787    \textcolor{comment}{// some people claim that the most significant bit might be used for alpha}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5788    \textcolor{comment}{// (possibly if an alpha-\/bit is set in the "{}image descriptor byte"{})}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5789    \textcolor{comment}{// but that only made 16bit test images completely translucent..}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5790    \textcolor{comment}{// so let's treat all 15 and 16bit TGAs as RGB with no alpha.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5791 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5792 }

\DoxyCodeLine{5977       \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5978          \textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char} temp = tga\_pixel[0];}
\DoxyCodeLine{5979          tga\_pixel[0] = tga\_pixel[2];}
\DoxyCodeLine{5980          tga\_pixel[2] = temp;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5981          tga\_pixel += tga\_comp;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5982       \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5983    \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5984 }
\DoxyCodeLine{5985    \textcolor{comment}{// convert to target component count}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5986    \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (req\_comp \&\& req\_comp != tga\_comp)}
\DoxyCodeLine{5987       tga\_data = stbi\_\_convert\_format(tga\_data, tga\_comp, req\_comp, tga\_width, tga\_height);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5988 }
\DoxyCodeLine{5989    \textcolor{comment}{//   the things I do to get rid of an error message, and yet keep}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5990    \textcolor{comment}{//   Microsoft's C compilers happy... [8\string^(}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5991    tga\_palette\_start = tga\_palette\_len = tga\_palette\_bits =}
\DoxyCodeLine{5992          tga\_x\_origin = tga\_y\_origin = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5993    STBI\_NOTUSED(tga\_palette\_start);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5994    \textcolor{comment}{//   OK, done}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5995    \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} tga\_data;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5996 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5997 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5998 }
\DoxyCodeLine{5999 \textcolor{comment}{// *************************************************************************************************}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6000 \textcolor{comment}{// Photoshop PSD loader -\/-\/ PD by Thatcher Ulrich, integration by Nicolas Schulz, tweaked by STB}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6001 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6002 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#ifndef STBI\_NO\_PSD}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6003 \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} stbi\_\_psd\_test(stbi\_\_context *s)}
\DoxyCodeLine{6004 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6005    \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} r = (stbi\_\_get32be(s) == 0x38425053);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6006    stbi\_\_rewind(s);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6007    \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} r;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6008 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6009 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6010 \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} stbi\_\_psd\_decode\_rle(stbi\_\_context *s, stbi\_uc *p, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} pixelCount)}
\DoxyCodeLine{6011 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6012    \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} count, nleft, len;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6013 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6014    count = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6015    \textcolor{keywordflow}{while} ((nleft = pixelCount -\/ count) > 0) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6016       len = stbi\_\_get8(s);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6017       \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (len == 128) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6018          \textcolor{comment}{// No-\/op.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6019       \} \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (len < 128) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6020          \textcolor{comment}{// Copy next len+1 bytes literally.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6021          len++;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6022          \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (len > nleft) \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} 0; \textcolor{comment}{// corrupt data}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6023          count += len;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6024          \textcolor{keywordflow}{while} (len) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6025             *p = stbi\_\_get8(s);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6026             p += 4;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6027             len-\/-\/;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6028          \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6029       \} \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (len > 128) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6030          stbi\_uc   val;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6031          \textcolor{comment}{// Next -\/len+1 bytes in the dest are replicated from next source byte.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6032          \textcolor{comment}{// (Interpret len as a negative 8-\/bit int.)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6033          len = 257 -\/ len;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6034          \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (len > nleft) \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} 0; \textcolor{comment}{// corrupt data}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6035          val = stbi\_\_get8(s);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6036          count += len;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6037          \textcolor{keywordflow}{while} (len) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6038             *p = val;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6039             p += 4;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6040             len-\/-\/;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6041          \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6042       \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6043    \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6044 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6045    \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6046 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6047 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6048 \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} *stbi\_\_psd\_load(stbi\_\_context *s, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} *x, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} *y, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} *comp, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} req\_comp, stbi\_\_result\_info *ri, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} bpc)}
\DoxyCodeLine{6049 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6050    \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} pixelCount;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6051    \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} channelCount, compression;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6052    \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} channel, i;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6053    \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} bitdepth;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6054    \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} w,h;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6055    stbi\_uc *out;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6056    STBI\_NOTUSED(ri);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6057 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6058    \textcolor{comment}{// Check identifier}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6059    \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (stbi\_\_get32be(s) != 0x38425053)   \textcolor{comment}{// "{}8BPS"{}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6060       \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} stbi\_\_errpuc(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}not PSD"{}}, \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}Corrupt PSD image"{}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{6061 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6062    \textcolor{comment}{// Check file type version.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6063    \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (stbi\_\_get16be(s) != 1)}
\DoxyCodeLine{6064       \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} stbi\_\_errpuc(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}wrong version"{}}, \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}Unsupported version of PSD image"{}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{6065 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6066    \textcolor{comment}{// Skip 6 reserved bytes.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6067    stbi\_\_skip(s, 6 );}
\DoxyCodeLine{6068 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6069    \textcolor{comment}{// Read the number of channels (R, G, B, A, etc).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6070    channelCount = stbi\_\_get16be(s);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6071    \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (channelCount < 0 || channelCount > 16)}
\DoxyCodeLine{6072       \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} stbi\_\_errpuc(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}wrong channel count"{}}, \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}Unsupported number of channels in PSD image"{}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{6073 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6074    \textcolor{comment}{// Read the rows and columns of the image.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6075    h = stbi\_\_get32be(s);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6076    w = stbi\_\_get32be(s);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6077 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6078    \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (h > STBI\_MAX\_DIMENSIONS) \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} stbi\_\_errpuc(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}too large"{}},\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}Very large image (corrupt?)"{}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{6079    \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (w > STBI\_MAX\_DIMENSIONS) \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} stbi\_\_errpuc(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}too large"{}},\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}Very large image (corrupt?)"{}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{6080 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6081    \textcolor{comment}{// Make sure the depth is 8 bits.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6082    bitdepth = stbi\_\_get16be(s);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6083    \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (bitdepth != 8 \&\& bitdepth != 16)}
\DoxyCodeLine{6084       \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} stbi\_\_errpuc(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}unsupported bit depth"{}}, \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}PSD bit depth is not 8 or 16 bit"{}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{6085 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6086    \textcolor{comment}{// Make sure the color mode is RGB.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6087    \textcolor{comment}{// Valid options are:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6088    \textcolor{comment}{//   0: Bitmap}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6089    \textcolor{comment}{//   1: Grayscale}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6090    \textcolor{comment}{//   2: Indexed color}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6091    \textcolor{comment}{//   3: RGB color}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6092    \textcolor{comment}{//   4: CMYK color}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6093    \textcolor{comment}{//   7: Multichannel}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6094    \textcolor{comment}{//   8: Duotone}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6095    \textcolor{comment}{//   9: Lab color}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6096    \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (stbi\_\_get16be(s) != 3)}
\DoxyCodeLine{6097       \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} stbi\_\_errpuc(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}wrong color format"{}}, \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}PSD is not in RGB color format"{}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{6098 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6099    \textcolor{comment}{// Skip the Mode Data.  (It's the palette for indexed color; other info for other modes.)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6100    stbi\_\_skip(s,stbi\_\_get32be(s) );}
\DoxyCodeLine{6101 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6102    \textcolor{comment}{// Skip the image resources.  (resolution, pen tool paths, etc)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6103    stbi\_\_skip(s, stbi\_\_get32be(s) );}
\DoxyCodeLine{6104 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6105    \textcolor{comment}{// Skip the reserved data.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6106    stbi\_\_skip(s, stbi\_\_get32be(s) );}
\DoxyCodeLine{6107 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6108    \textcolor{comment}{// Find out if the data is compressed.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6109    \textcolor{comment}{// Known values:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6110    \textcolor{comment}{//   0: no compression}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6111    \textcolor{comment}{//   1: RLE compressed}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6112    compression = stbi\_\_get16be(s);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6113    \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (compression > 1)}
\DoxyCodeLine{6114       \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} stbi\_\_errpuc(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}bad compression"{}}, \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}PSD has an unknown compression format"{}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{6115 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6116    \textcolor{comment}{// Check size}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6117    \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (!stbi\_\_mad3sizes\_valid(4, w, h, 0))}
\DoxyCodeLine{6118       \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} stbi\_\_errpuc(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}too large"{}}, \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}Corrupt PSD"{}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{6119 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6120    \textcolor{comment}{// Create the destination image.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6121 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6122    \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (!compression \&\& bitdepth == 16 \&\& bpc == 16) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6123       out = (stbi\_uc *) stbi\_\_malloc\_mad3(8, w, h, 0);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6124       ri-\/>bits\_per\_channel = 16;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6125    \} \textcolor{keywordflow}{else}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6126       out = (stbi\_uc *) stbi\_\_malloc(4 * w*h);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6127 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6128    \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (!out) \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} stbi\_\_errpuc(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}outofmem"{}}, \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}Out of memory"{}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{6129    pixelCount = w*h;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6130 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6131    \textcolor{comment}{// Initialize the data to zero.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6132    \textcolor{comment}{//memset( out, 0, pixelCount * 4 );}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6133 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6134    \textcolor{comment}{// Finally, the image data.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6135    \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (compression) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6136       \textcolor{comment}{// RLE as used by .PSD and .TIFF}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6137       \textcolor{comment}{// Loop until you get the number of unpacked bytes you are expecting:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6138       \textcolor{comment}{//     Read the next source byte into n.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6139       \textcolor{comment}{//     If n is between 0 and 127 inclusive, copy the next n+1 bytes literally.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6140       \textcolor{comment}{//     Else if n is between -\/127 and -\/1 inclusive, copy the next byte -\/n+1 times.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6141       \textcolor{comment}{//     Else if n is 128, noop.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6142       \textcolor{comment}{// Endloop}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6143 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6144       \textcolor{comment}{// The RLE-\/compressed data is preceded by a 2-\/byte data count for each row in the data,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6145       \textcolor{comment}{// which we're going to just skip.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6146       stbi\_\_skip(s, h * channelCount * 2 );}
\DoxyCodeLine{6147 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6148       \textcolor{comment}{// Read the RLE data by channel.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6149       \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (channel = 0; channel < 4; channel++) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6150          stbi\_uc *p;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6151 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6152          p = out+channel;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6153          \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (channel >= channelCount) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6154             \textcolor{comment}{// Fill this channel with default data.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6155             \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (i = 0; i < pixelCount; i++, p += 4)}
\DoxyCodeLine{6156                *p = (channel == 3 ? 255 : 0);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6157          \} \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6158             \textcolor{comment}{// Read the RLE data.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6159             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (!stbi\_\_psd\_decode\_rle(s, p, pixelCount)) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6160                STBI\_FREE(out);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6161                \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} stbi\_\_errpuc(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}corrupt"{}}, \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}bad RLE data"{}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{6162             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6163          \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6164       \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6165 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6166    \} \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6167       \textcolor{comment}{// We're at the raw image data.  It's each channel in order (Red, Green, Blue, Alpha, ...)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6168       \textcolor{comment}{// where each channel consists of an 8-\/bit (or 16-\/bit) value for each pixel in the image.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6169 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6170       \textcolor{comment}{// Read the data by channel.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6171       \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (channel = 0; channel < 4; channel++) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6172          \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (channel >= channelCount) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6173             \textcolor{comment}{// Fill this channel with default data.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6174             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (bitdepth == 16 \&\& bpc == 16) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6175                stbi\_\_uint16 *q = ((stbi\_\_uint16 *) out) + channel;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6176                stbi\_\_uint16 val = channel == 3 ? 65535 : 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6177                \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (i = 0; i < pixelCount; i++, q += 4)}
\DoxyCodeLine{6178                   *q = val;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6179             \} \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6180                stbi\_uc *p = out+channel;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6181                stbi\_uc val = channel == 3 ? 255 : 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6182                \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (i = 0; i < pixelCount; i++, p += 4)}
\DoxyCodeLine{6183                   *p = val;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6184             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6185          \} \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6186             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (ri-\/>bits\_per\_channel == 16) \{    \textcolor{comment}{// output bpc}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6187                stbi\_\_uint16 *q = ((stbi\_\_uint16 *) out) + channel;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6188                \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (i = 0; i < pixelCount; i++, q += 4)}
\DoxyCodeLine{6189                   *q = (stbi\_\_uint16) stbi\_\_get16be(s);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6190             \} \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6191                stbi\_uc *p = out+channel;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6192                \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (bitdepth == 16) \{  \textcolor{comment}{// input bpc}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6193                   \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (i = 0; i < pixelCount; i++, p += 4)}
\DoxyCodeLine{6194                      *p = (stbi\_uc) (stbi\_\_get16be(s) >> 8);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6195                \} \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6196                   \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (i = 0; i < pixelCount; i++, p += 4)}
\DoxyCodeLine{6197                      *p = stbi\_\_get8(s);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6198                \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6199             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6200          \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6201       \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6202    \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6203 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6204    \textcolor{comment}{// remove weird white matte from PSD}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6205    \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (channelCount >= 4) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6206       \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (ri-\/>bits\_per\_channel == 16) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6207          \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (i=0; i < w*h; ++i) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6208             stbi\_\_uint16 *pixel = (stbi\_\_uint16 *) out + 4*i;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6209             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (pixel[3] != 0 \&\& pixel[3] != 65535) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6210                \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} a = pixel[3] / 65535.0f;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6211                \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} ra = 1.0f / a;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6212                \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} inv\_a = 65535.0f * (1 -\/ ra);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6213                pixel[0] = (stbi\_\_uint16) (pixel[0]*ra + inv\_a);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6214                pixel[1] = (stbi\_\_uint16) (pixel[1]*ra + inv\_a);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6215                pixel[2] = (stbi\_\_uint16) (pixel[2]*ra + inv\_a);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6216             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6217          \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6218       \} \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6219          \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (i=0; i < w*h; ++i) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6220             \textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char} *pixel = out + 4*i;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6221             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (pixel[3] != 0 \&\& pixel[3] != 255) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6222                \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} a = pixel[3] / 255.0f;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6223                \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} ra = 1.0f / a;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6224                \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} inv\_a = 255.0f * (1 -\/ ra);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6225                pixel[0] = (\textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} char) (pixel[0]*ra + inv\_a);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6226                pixel[1] = (\textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} char) (pixel[1]*ra + inv\_a);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6227                pixel[2] = (\textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} char) (pixel[2]*ra + inv\_a);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6228             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6229          \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6230       \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6231    \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6232 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6233    \textcolor{comment}{// convert to desired output format}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6234    \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (req\_comp \&\& req\_comp != 4) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6235       \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (ri-\/>bits\_per\_channel == 16)}
\DoxyCodeLine{6236          out = (stbi\_uc *) stbi\_\_convert\_format16((stbi\_\_uint16 *) out, 4, req\_comp, w, h);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6237       \textcolor{keywordflow}{else}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6238          out = stbi\_\_convert\_format(out, 4, req\_comp, w, h);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6239       \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (out == NULL) \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} out; \textcolor{comment}{// stbi\_\_convert\_format frees input on failure}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6240    \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6241 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6242    \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (comp) *comp = 4;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6243    *y = h;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6244    *x = w;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6245 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6246    \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} out;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6247 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6248 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif}}

\DoxyCodeLine{6576 \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} stbi\_\_out\_gif\_code(stbi\_\_gif *g, stbi\_\_uint16 code)}
\DoxyCodeLine{6577 \{}

\DoxyCodeLine{6579    \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} idx;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6580 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6581    \textcolor{comment}{// recurse to decode the prefixes, since the linked-\/list is backwards,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6582    \textcolor{comment}{// and working backwards through an interleaved image would be nasty}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6583    \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (g-\/>codes[code].prefix >= 0)}
\DoxyCodeLine{6584       stbi\_\_out\_gif\_code(g, g-\/>codes[code].prefix);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6585 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6586    \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (g-\/>cur\_y >= g-\/>max\_y) \textcolor{keywordflow}{return};}
\DoxyCodeLine{6587 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6588    idx = g-\/>cur\_x + g-\/>cur\_y;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6589    p = \&g-\/>out[idx];}
\DoxyCodeLine{6590    g-\/>history[idx / 4] = 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6591 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6592    c = \&g-\/>color\_table[g-\/>codes[code].suffix * 4];}

\DoxyCodeLine{6594       p[0] = c[2];}
\DoxyCodeLine{6595       p[1] = c[1];}
\DoxyCodeLine{6596       p[2] = c[0];}
\DoxyCodeLine{6597       p[3] = c[3];}
\DoxyCodeLine{6598    \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6599    g-\/>cur\_x += 4;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6600 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6601    \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (g-\/>cur\_x >= g-\/>max\_x) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6602       g-\/>cur\_x = g-\/>start\_x;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6603       g-\/>cur\_y += g-\/>step;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6604 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6605       \textcolor{keywordflow}{while} (g-\/>cur\_y >= g-\/>max\_y \&\& g-\/>parse > 0) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6606          g-\/>step = (1 << g-\/>parse) * g-\/>line\_size;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6607          g-\/>cur\_y = g-\/>start\_y + (g-\/>step >> 1);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6608          -\/-\/g-\/>parse;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6609       \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6610    \}}

\DoxyCodeLine{6613 \textcolor{keyword}{static} stbi\_uc *stbi\_\_process\_gif\_raster(stbi\_\_context *s, stbi\_\_gif *g)}

\DoxyCodeLine{6617    stbi\_\_uint32 first;}

\DoxyCodeLine{6620 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6621    lzw\_cs = stbi\_\_get8(s);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6622    \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (lzw\_cs > 12) \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} NULL;}

\DoxyCodeLine{6625    codesize = lzw\_cs + 1;}

\DoxyCodeLine{6628    valid\_bits = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6629    \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (init\_code = 0; init\_code < clear; init\_code++) \{}

\DoxyCodeLine{6631       g-\/>codes[init\_code].first = (stbi\_uc) init\_code;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6632       g-\/>codes[init\_code].suffix = (stbi\_uc) init\_code;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6633    \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6634 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6635    \textcolor{comment}{// support no starting clear code}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6636    avail = clear+2;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6637    oldcode = -\/1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6638 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6639    len = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6640    \textcolor{keywordflow}{for}(;;) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6641       \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (valid\_bits < codesize) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6642          \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (len == 0) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6643             len = stbi\_\_get8(s); \textcolor{comment}{// start new block}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6644             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (len == 0)}
\DoxyCodeLine{6645                \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} g-\/>out;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6646          \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6647          -\/-\/len;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6648          bits |= (stbi\_\_int32) stbi\_\_get8(s) << valid\_bits;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6649          valid\_bits += 8;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6650       \} \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6651          stbi\_\_int32 code = bits \& codemask;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6652          bits >>= codesize;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6653          valid\_bits -\/= codesize;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6654          \textcolor{comment}{// @OPTIMIZE: is there some way we can accelerate the non-\/clear path?}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6655          \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (code == clear) \{  \textcolor{comment}{// clear code}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6656             codesize = lzw\_cs + 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6657             codemask = (1 << codesize) -\/ 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6658             avail = clear + 2;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6659             oldcode = -\/1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6660             first = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6661          \} \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (code == clear + 1) \{ \textcolor{comment}{// end of stream code}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6662             stbi\_\_skip(s, len);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6663             \textcolor{keywordflow}{while} ((len = stbi\_\_get8(s)) > 0)}
\DoxyCodeLine{6664                stbi\_\_skip(s,len);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6665             \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} g-\/>out;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6666          \} \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (code <= avail) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6667             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (first) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6668                \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} stbi\_\_errpuc(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}no clear code"{}}, \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}Corrupt GIF"{}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{6669             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6670 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6671             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (oldcode >= 0) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6672                p = \&g-\/>codes[avail++];}
\DoxyCodeLine{6673                \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (avail > 8192) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6674                   \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} stbi\_\_errpuc(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}too many codes"{}}, \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}Corrupt GIF"{}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{6675                \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6676 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6677                p-\/>prefix = (stbi\_\_int16) oldcode;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6678                p-\/>first = g-\/>codes[oldcode].first;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6679                p-\/>suffix = (code == avail) ? p-\/>first : g-\/>codes[code].first;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6680             \} \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (code == avail)}

\DoxyCodeLine{6684 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6685             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} ((avail \& codemask) == 0 \&\& avail <= 0x0FFF) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6686                codesize++;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6687                codemask = (1 << codesize) -\/ 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6688             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6689 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6690             oldcode = code;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6691          \} \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \{}

\DoxyCodeLine{6693          \}}

\DoxyCodeLine{6698 \textcolor{comment}{// this function is designed to support animated gifs, although stb\_image doesn't support it}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6699 \textcolor{comment}{// two back is the image from two frames ago, used for a very specific disposal format}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6700 \textcolor{keyword}{static} stbi\_uc *stbi\_\_gif\_load\_next(stbi\_\_context *s, stbi\_\_gif *g, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} *comp, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} req\_comp, stbi\_uc *two\_back)}

\DoxyCodeLine{6717       g-\/>history = (stbi\_uc *) stbi\_\_malloc(pcount);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6718       \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (!g-\/>out || !g-\/>background || !g-\/>history)}

\DoxyCodeLine{6723       \textcolor{comment}{// color refers to the color that was there the previous frame.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{6731       pcount = g-\/>w * g-\/>h;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6732 }

\DoxyCodeLine{7053 \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} stbi\_\_hdr\_convert(\textcolor{keywordtype}{float} *output, stbi\_uc *input, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} req\_comp)}
\DoxyCodeLine{7054 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{7055    \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} ( input[3] != 0 ) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{7056       \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} f1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{7057       \textcolor{comment}{// Exponent}}
\DoxyCodeLine{7058       f1 = (float) \mbox{\hyperlink{group__core__func__common_gac3010e0a0c35a1b514540f2fb579c58c}{ldexp}}(1.0f, input[3] -\/ (\textcolor{keywordtype}{int})(128 + 8));}
\DoxyCodeLine{7059       \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (req\_comp <= 2)}
\DoxyCodeLine{7060          output[0] = (input[0] + input[1] + input[2]) * f1 / 3;}
\DoxyCodeLine{7061       \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{7062          output[0] = input[0] * f1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{7063          output[1] = input[1] * f1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{7064          output[2] = input[2] * f1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{7065       \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{7066       \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (req\_comp == 2) output[1] = 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{7067       \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (req\_comp == 4) output[3] = 1;}

\DoxyCodeLine{7069       \textcolor{keywordflow}{switch} (req\_comp) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{7070          \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} 4: output[3] = 1; \textcolor{comment}{/* fallthrough */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{7071          \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} 3: output[0] = output[1] = output[2] = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{7072                  \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{7073          \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} 2: output[1] = 1; \textcolor{comment}{/* fallthrough */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{7074          \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} 1: output[0] = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{7075                  \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{7076       \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{7077    \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{7078 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{7079 }
